图2原始红和早幼红细胞
1.原始红细胞呈类圆形，胞浆嗜碱深蓝色，边缘部有伪
足突起，核周有环核淡染带。核圆形，染色质呈细颗粒状，
核仁1~4个2.早幼红细胞胞体圆形、椭圆形、胞浆嗜
碱，染深蓝色。核圆形，染色质粗点状，有少许聚集，无
核仁3.双核早幼红细胞
Fig.2 Pronormoblasts and Basophilic Normoblasts
1.Pronormoblasts The cells are similar to round in
shape.The basophilic cytoplasm is dark blue with
prominences as pseudopodia at the periphery and a
perinuclear pallid zone.The nuclei are round with
fine and granular chromatin andI-4 nucleoli 2. Ba-
sophilic normoblasts They are round or elliptic in
shape. The basophilic cytoplasm is stained dark blue.
Roundnucleicontain coarse-granular chromatinwithout
nucleole 3.Basophilicnormoblast with double nuclei
图3中幼红细胞
1.花瓣形中幼红细胞
其余均为中幼红细胞胞体呈不规则形，较早幼红细胞小
胞浆从嗜碱蓝染到出现啫多色性。核圆形，染色质聚集成
小块状
Fig.3 Polychromatic Normoblasts
1.Polychromatic normoblasts with petaling nuclei
The rest are all polychromatic. The cells are irregular
in shape and smaller than basophilic normoblasts.The
color of cytoplasm goes from deeply basophilic to
polychromatic.The chromatin of round nuclei is like
small coarse clumps
图4晚幼红细胞
胞体类圆形，胞浆已接近成熟红细胞的红色，个别尚有少
许蓝色。核呈圆形、染色质致密
1.晚幼红浆中出现碎裂的核小体2.晚幼红胞浆中出现红
色的嗜苯胺蓝颗粒3.花瓣形晚幼红细胞
Fig.4 Orthochromatic Normoblasts
The cells are similar to round in shape.Redish cy-
toplasm is similar to that ofmature erythrocytes.In
few cells the cytoplasm shows a little blue yet.The
nuclei are round with compact chromatin.
1.Orthochromaticnormoblast with fragmentednu-
cleosome in the cytoplasm 2.Orthochromaticnormo-
blast with red azurophilic granules in the cytoplasm
3.Orthochromatic normoblasts with petalingnuclei

图5原始粒细胞（1、I型）
1.原始粒细胞Ⅱ型胞体为圆形或类圆形。胞浆呈天蓝色，
边缘稍深。浆中有少许细小的嗜苯胺蓝颗粒。核居中或偏
在，染色质呈细沙粒状。核仁2-5个，染灰色
余者为1型
Fig.5Myeloblasts (Type I andIl)
1.Type Il myeloblasts They are round or elliptic in
shape. The blue cytoplasm has more deeply stained
margin.A few azurophilic granules can be found in
the cytoplasm.The nuclei are in the center or eccen-
tricwith fineehromatin and 2-5greynucleoli (type
I).The other cells are type I myeloblasts
图6早幼粒细胞
胞体比原粒大，圆形或不规则形。胞浆比原粒为淡，呈淡
蓝色、有淡染的初浆区，含有多少不等的非特异性颗粒，有
的聚集成堆或散在于核上。核圆形、椭圆形，染色质已开
始聚集。核仁0-2个
Fig.6Promyelocytes
The cells are bigger than myeloblasts in size,round or
irregular in shape.Light blue cytoplasm with lightly
stained archoplasm zone contains non-specific granules
in different number: some granules are aggregating in
clumps or scattering on the nuclei. The nuclei are
round or elliptic with aggregated chromatin and 0-2
nucleoli
图7早幼粒细胞
图中均为早幼粒细胞的各种形态
Fig.7Promyelocytes
All the cells are promyelocytes in different shapes

图8中性中幼粒细胞
胞体为圆形并变小。胞浆淡紫红色，较早期的中幼粒还有
蓝色基调，含有较淡的紫红色特异性颗粒。核椭圆或有凹
陷，常偏于一侧，染色质浓集
Fig.8NeutrophilicMyelocytes
The round cells are going smaller.The cytoplasm is
light purplish-red,or blue in the earlier-stage cells.
with many specificpurplish-red granules.The nuclei
are ellipticorcavate andfrequently located inone side
of the cells with dense chromatin.
图9中性晚幼粒细胞
胞体为圆形，胞浆淡红色，含有小的淡紫红色特异性颗粒。
核一侧明显凹陷呈肾形、花生形或有切迹的肾形。染色质
粗糙成块
Fig.9NeutrophilicMetamyelocytes
The round cells have pale-red cytoplasm containing
many small specific purplish-red granules.One side of
the nuclei are obviously cavate presenting reniform
and peanut-like shapes.The chromatin is coarse as
clumps.
图10中性杆状核粒细胞和中性分叶核粒细胞

多的特异性颗粒。核呈带状弯曲，染色质呈块状2.双核
中性杆状核粒细胞3.中性分叶核粒细胞核与核之间有
细丝相连或完全断离、胞浆中含有细小的特异性颗粒4.中
性分叶核粒细胞浆中含有的黑褐色颗粒为中毒颗粒
Fig.10 Neutrophilic Stab and Segmented Cells
1.Neutrophilic stab cellsThe cells are round in shape
with many specific granules in the pale-red cytoplasm.
Thenuclei show the shape ofband with the chroma-
tin as clumps 2. Stab cell with double nuclei 3.Neu-
trophilic segmented cellsThe lobes ofnuclei are con
nectedwith eachother through filamentsor separated
completely.The cytoplasm contains specific and fine
granules 4.The cytoplasm contains dark-brown toxic
particles.

缺铁性贫血
缺铁性贫血（Irondeficiencyanemia，IDA）是由于体内合成血红蛋白的铁质不足导致红细胞生成障碍所致的
小细胞低色素性贫血。成人慢性失血是主要原因。
血象红细胞与血红蛋白均减少，但血红蛋白的减少比前者更为明显，呈典型的小细胞低色素性贫血。网织
红细胞大多正常，成熟红细胞中心淡染区明显扩大，易见畸形红细胞。白细胞和血小板一般正常。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃，红细胞系统明显增生，以中、晚幼红细胞增生为主。细胞胞体较小，胞浆量少，
边缘不规则呈毛刺状，胞浆因血红蛋白不足而嗜碱色调明显，甚至晚幼红细胞可呈嗜多色性。细胞核小而致密，
某些晚幼红细胞由于胞核浓缩、胞浆极少颇似小淋巴细胞。粒系与巨核系正常。细胞内、外铁减少或消失。成熟
红细胞中心淡染区明显扩大。
Iron Deficiency Anemia
Iron deficiency anemia (IDA)is a kind of microcytic and hypochromic anemia.IDA occurs when
21
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
hemoglobin synthesis is decreased,which is resulted from inadequate body iron stores.In adults.chronic
bloodlossismorefrequentlyresponsibleforIDA.
Hemogram Both red blood cells（RBC)and hemoglobin （HGB)reduce,and the decrease of
hemoglobin is more obvious than of RBC,so that the cells tend to be microcyticand hypochromic.
Reticulocyte count is often normal.Hypochromatic zone ofmature red cells ismarkedly enlarged.The
white blood cell(WBC)and theplatelet（PLT)countareusuallynormal.
MyelogramThemarrowiscellularwitherythroidhyperplasia.Polychromaticandorthochromatic
eries as burrs is obviously basophilic,even polychromatic in orthochromaticnormoblasts because of
decreased hemoglobin.The nuclei are small and dense. Some orthochromatic normoblasts are similar to
small lymphocytes because of the dense nuclei and scanty cytoplasm. Granulocytic and megakaryocytic
lineages are normal.The intracellular and extracellular iron granules becomerare or absent.Hypochromatic
zone of mature red cells is markedly enlarged.

成熟红细胞大小不等，畸形，中心淡染区明显扩大

巨幼细胞贫血
由于叶酸、维生素B缺乏或吸收障碍，细胞内DNA合成障碍而引起大细胞贫血，同时骨髓中出现巨幼细
胞，故称巨幼细胞贫血（Megaloblasticanemias，MA）。除贫血症状外，可有食欲不振、腹泻、舌痛、舌质绛红。
如果B，缺乏，尚可有下肢对称性深部感觉消失，腱反射减弱或消失等亚急性脊髓联合变性的症状和体征。
血象红细胞与血红蛋白均减少，尤以红细胞减少更为明显，易见大的椭圆形红细胞。白细胞正常或减少，
中性粒细胞有分叶过多现象，可见幼红和幼粒细胞。网织红细胞正常或轻度升高。血小板可减少。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃，幼红细胞百分比常大于40%，以中幼红和早幼红细胞为主，并出现较多的巨
幼红细胞，常大于10%。胞体较大，核染色质疏松。由于胞浆内核糖核酸及蛋白质合成未受影响，故细胞核发育
落后于细胞浆。易见染色质小体（Howell-Jolly小体）及嗜多色性红细胞。粒细胞从早幼粒起就开始有巨幼改变，
但主要是中、晚幼粒及杆状核粒细胞呈巨幼变，分叶核粒细胞分叶过多，有时可达10个叶以上。巨核细胞可见
到分叶过多现象。早期以粒细胞系统改变为主，恢复期时粒细胞系统改变的恢复慢于红细胞系统。
MegaloblasticAnemias
Megaloblastic anemias (MA)are disorders caused by impaired DNA synthesis,which are most
commonly due to a deficiency or malabsorption of folateorVitamin B(cobalamin).When symptoms
present in deficiency ofVitamin B. such as subacute combined degeneration of the spinal cordresulting
in symmetrical lossof deep sensation of lower limbs and tendon reflexes.
HemogramBothRBCand hemoglobinreduce,and thereductionin RBCis more obvious than in
hemoglobin.Large ovalocytes can be seen easily.White blood cell count is normal or reduces,and
Reticulocyte count is normal or increases slightly.Platelet count can be decreased.
MyelogramThe marrow is cellular with erythroid hyperplasia.Erythroblasts are usually more
than 40%,basophilicandpolychromaticnormoblasts arein the majority.Megaloblasts canbe seenand
are usually more than 10%.Megaloblasts are large and have loose chromatin,andnuclei develop later
than cytoplasm because synthesis ofRNAs and proteins in the cytoplasm is normal. Chromatin remnants
(Howell-Jolly bodies)and polychromatic erythrocytes can be easily observed.Neutrophils begin to show
megaloblastic change from promyelocyte stage,butmore obviousinmyelocytes,metamyelocytesand stab
erythrocyticlineage disappearmore quickly than myelocyticlineage during therecovery stage.

双相性贫血
巨幼细胞性贫血合并有铁的缺乏，临床表现为巨幼细胞性贫血或缺铁性贫血，因铁的缺乏可使血红蛋白合成
发生障碍从而掩盖了红细胞系的巨幼变，血清铁、铁蛋白减少，血清叶酸和/或B2缺乏。
血象贫血程度轻重不一，严重者可有全血细胞减少，红细胞大小不等，部分成熟红细胞中空淡染区扩大。
骨髓象红细胞系增生活跃，幼红细胞巨幼变可不明显，胞体偏小，但缺乏缺铁性贫血的典型表现，细胞内
铁减少。粒细胞系统及巨核细胞系统可有巨幼变。
Bisphasic Anemias
It isrefered to megaloblastic anemias coexistingwith iron deficiency,which presents asmegaloblastic
anemias or iron deficiency anemia.Theobstruction ofhemoglobulin synthesis resulted from iron defi-
ciency conceals the megaloblasticchange of erythrocytes.Serum iron and ferritin are decreased and serum
folic acid and /or Vitamin Bare insufficient.
Hemogram Anemia is varing in degree. Pancytopenia,anisocytosis and enlargement of pale center
oferythrocytescanbeseenin severecases.
MyelogramErythrocyticlineagearehypercellular,megaloblasticchangeof erythroblastsmaybe
indistinct.Erythroblasts are smallerwithout the typical features of iron deficiency anemia.The intrac-
ellular iron is decreased. Granulocytic and megakaryocyticlineagemay have megaloblasticchanges.

遗传性球形红细胞增多症
遗传性球形红细胞增多症（Hereditaryspherocytosis，HS）是红细胞膜先天性缺陷所致的溶血性贫血，为常
染色体显性遗传，男女均可发病。主要的临床表现是贫血、黄疽和脾大。多在童年或青年时期发病，也有中年时
期才出现症状。血象中小球形红细胞增多为其特征，红细胞脆性增加。本病可合并胆石症和小腿慢性溃疡，脾切
除疗效良好。
血象、红细胞和血红蛋白轻至中度减少，呈正细胞正色素性贫血。可见较多胞体较小、染色深、中心淡染区
消失的小球形红细胞，一般超过20%～30%，甚至达到60%～70%（正常人<5%）。易见嗜多色性红细胞和幼红
细胞。网织红细胞增多，可高达5%～50%，但在溶血危象时减少或消失。白细胞正常或稍增多，偶见晚幼粒细胞。
血小板计数一般正常。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃，粒红比值降低。红细胞系统增生旺盛，各阶段幼红细胞均增多，但以中、晚幼
红细胞为主。小球形红细胞增多。粒细胞及巨核细胞系统正常。
Hereditary Spherocytosis
Hereditary spherocytosis(Hs)whichinheritedas an autosomal dominant trait isakindofhemolytic
anemia as a result ofabnormality in the membrane oferythrocytes.The disease may occur in men and
women.The most frequent clinical manifestations are anemia,jaundice and splenomegaly.The onset of
HS typically is in childhood or the youth, also in middle age.Microspherocytes on blood films are
and chronic leg skin ulceration. Splenectomyis an effective treatment in the majority ofpatients.
Hemogram Mostpatients have mild or moderate anemia which is normocytic and normochromic.
Blood films reveal microspherocytes that are deeply stained and lack of pale center.These cells are more
than20%~30%,even 60%-70%(<5%in normal).Erythroblasts and polychromatic erythrocytes can be
phils are normal or slightly increased, and metamyelocytes are casually seen.Platelet count is usually
normal.
erythroidprecursors（G/Eratio)is decreased.Erythroblasts in differently developed stages increase with
the majority ofpolychromatic and orthochromatic normoblasts.Microspherocytesare increased in number.
Granulocytic and megakaryocyticlineages are normal.

遗传性椭圆形红细胞增多症
遗传性椭圆形红细胞增多症（Hereditaryelliptocytosis，HE）是一组异质性家族遗传性溶血病。其特点是
外周血存在大量的椭圆形成熟红细胞，绝大多数大于25%，一般可达60%～90%，为常染色体隐性遗传。多数为
杂合子，少数为纯合子。杂合子遗传性椭圆形红细胞增多症一般无贫血和脾大，仅有轻度贫血，网织红细胞计数
一般低于3%
血象易见红细胞呈椭圆形、棒状，可见少数嗜多色性球形红细胞，偶见幼红细胞。有溶血时网织红细胞增
高。血小板及白细胞一般正常
骨髓象大致正常，成熟红细胞形态同血象。
Hereditary Elliptocytosis
Hereditary elliptocytosis(HE)is a term thatrefers to a group of heterogenetic family-inherited
disorders characterized byplenty of elliptocytes onperipheral blood smear,which exceed25%in the
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
majority ofpatients andgenerallyup to 60%~90%.Itis anautosomalrecessiveinherited disease.Most
patientsareheterozygotes whileminority arehomozygotes.Patients withheterozygotichereditary
elliptocytosis generally have no anemia and splenomegaly,occasionally present with mild anemia,and
theirreticulocytesarelower than3%.
HemogramErythrocytes are elliptic orrod-like.A few spherocytes and few erythroblasts can also
be found.Reticular cells increasewhen hemolysis occurs.PLT and WBC counts arenormal.
MyelogramThe marrow is almost normal. The morphous of mature erythrocytes is the same as
that in theperipheralblood.

自身免疫性溶血性贫血
自身免疫性溶血性贫血（Autoimmunehemolyticanemia，AIHA）是由于免疫功能异常而产生了自身抗
体，当抗体和/或补体与自身正常红细胞表面的抗原结合或激活了补体促使红细胞破坏加速所引起的一组溶血性
贫血。
原发性温抗体型自身免疫性溶血性贫血，发病多为女性。临床表现以溶血和贫血为主。急性者起病急骤，寒战、
高热、贫血、黄痘、呕吐、腹泻、腹痛甚至昏迷，偶有血红蛋白尿。慢性者起病缓慢，有头晕、乏力等贫血症状。
血象红细胞和血红蛋白不同程度减少，球形红细胞和嗜多色性红细胞常增多，可出现幼红细胞。网织红细
胞一般明显增高。白细胞总数正常或增高，可出现幼粒细胞。血小板计数正常，偶尔显著减少（Evans综合征）。
当发生再生障碍危象时，贫血加重，甚至血象呈全血细胞减少，网织红细胞极度减少或消失。
骨髓象骨髓有核细胞增生明显活跃，以红系增生为主，粒红比值降低，有时由于红系过度增生引起相对性
叶酸缺乏而导致幼红细胞发生巨幼样变，也可有再生障碍危象的骨髓象。
抗人球蛋白（Coombs）试验是诊断本病的最主要依据，直接试验阳性，主要是抗IgG和C3型，间接试验
可为阳性或阴性。
Autoimmune HemolyticAnemia
Autoimmune hemolyticanemia(AIHA)is characterized by shortenedred cell survival and the
presence of autoantibodies directed against autologousred blood cells.Erythrocyte autoantibodies in
AIHA are pathogenic.
Acquired hemolyticanemia due towarm-reactingautoantibodies is mostly diagnosed in female.
Clinicalfeaturesusuallyarehemolysisandanemia.Acutehemolysismaybe associatedwitharapidonset,
high fever,chills,anemia,jaundice,vomiting,diarrhea,abdominal pain,even coma and sometimes
hemoglobinuria.Chronic hemolysis has a slow onset and shows those symptoms of anemia such as
dizziness and fatigue.
HemogramPatients with AIHA present with anemia,the severity ofwhich canvary from life-
threatening to very mild.Spherocytes,polychromatic erythrocytes and erythroblasts can be found.The
reticulocyte countisincreased obviously.The white bloodcell count is normal orincreased,and immature
granulocytes can be seen.Theplateletcountisnormal.Severe thrombocytopenia canbe associated with
AIHA,which is termed as Evans Syndrome.Unusually when aplastic crisis occur,severe anemia,
pancytopenia,decreasedreticulocytes andmarrow erythroid aplasia may be found.
MyelogramMarrow examination usuallyrevealserythroidhyperplasia,andtheratioofgranalocytic/
Aplastic crisiscasuallypresents.
A positive direct antiglobulin reaction(Coombs test),mainly anti-IgG and anti-C3 types is themost
important envidence for the dliagnosis,Indirect antiglobulin reaction may be positive or negative.

微血管病性溶血性贫血
微血管病性溶血性贫血（Microangiophathichemolyticanemia，MHA）是指在微血管病变的基础上，由
于机械性因素使红细胞在微血管内破裂，导致溶血性贫血。血象中出现盔形、棘形、三角形、微小球形红细胞碎
片和其他畸形红细胞是其特点。常伴有血小板减少，见于DIC、TTP、HUS等疾病，也见于心源性溶血性贫血。
在原发病的症状和体征的基础上，迅速出现贫血、黄疽、程度不等的皮肤黏膜出血，血红蛋白尿。
血象血红蛋白不同程度下降，出现各种畸形和碎片红细胞，多在3%～5%以上，网织红细胞增多，常出现
幼红、幼粒细胞。
骨髓象骨髓有核细胞增生活跃，以红系增生为主，并有畸形和碎片红细胞。
Microangiophathic HemolyticAnemia
The termmicroangiopathichemolytic anemia(MHA)refers to the hemolytic anemia characterized by
the fragmentation of red cells because of their mechanical damage as they pass through abnormal small
35
图谱

vessles.Helmet cells,prick cells,triangular cells and microglobular erythrocyticfragments and other
abnormal erythrocytes present in the blood smear.It occurs in DIC,TTP and HUS usually with
thrombocytopenia.MHA is also seen in cardiac-originated hemolytic anemia.Clinical manifestations are
rapidly progressive anemia,jaundice,dermal and mucous hemorrhage in different degree,and hemoglo-
binuria following those of the primary disorders.
HemogramThe descent degree of hemoglobulin isvaryingwith abnormal and fragmented erythrocytes,
which areoften over 3%~5%.Reticulocytesareelevated.Erythroblasts andimmaturegranulocytesare

fragmented erythrocytes can be seen.

急性造血功能停滞
急性造血功能停滞（Acutehemopoieticarrest）又称急性纯红细胞再生障碍（Acutepureredcellaplasia）、
急性幼红细胞减少症（Acuteerythroblastopenia）、获得性急性红细胞造血功能低下（Acquiredacuteeryth-
ropoietichypoplasia）、再生障碍性危象（Aplasticcrisis）等。
本病特点：停滞前常有高热，迅速出现苍白、乏力；有不同程度的贫血，可有白细胞和/或血小板减
少，网织红细胞减少或阙如；骨髓中红细胞系统显著减少或消失，并可见巨大原始红细胞。有些病例并非
单纯性红细胞再生障碍，也可不同程度地累及粒系和巨核系。
血象血红蛋白波动在（25~110）g/L，半数病例小于50g/L。网织红细胞减少或消失。白细胞总数可正
常、减低或增高，波动范围为（0.9~16.2）×10/L，分类大多正常，偶见淋巴细胞增高。白细胞有时低至
0.4×10/L。中性粒细胞减少或阙如。血小板一般正常，也可减少。恢复期网织红细胞升高，同时出现幼稚粒
细胞和/或中、晚幼红细胞。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分大多数正常，少数可增高或减低。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃，少数明显活跃，也可增生低下。由于红系显著减少或消失，粒红比值相对升高，
有时计数500个有核细胞未见到幼红细胞。巨核细胞多少不一。
典型特征是骨髓片尾部及边缘可见巨大的原始红细胞，它是急性造血功能停滞的标志之一，约90%病例有
巨大的原始红细胞。它呈圆形、椭圆形或不规则形，小者18um×22um，大者可达34μm×36um。浆深蓝或
蓝色，不透明，量少，有环核淡染带，周边部常有一至数个钝形突起，可有数个空泡，偶可见到少量嗜苯胺蓝
颗粒。核圆形或椭圆形，染色质呈细点网状。有时较正常原始红细胞的染色质为粗，呈紫红色。核仁常巨大或
隐约不清，偶有空泡。此外，尚能见到此种红细胞的丝球期分裂象和多核巨大原始红细胞，也可见到异常有丝
分裂细胞。巨大原始红细胞PAS染色一般为阴性，偶有阳性。此外约70%病例可见到巨大的网状细胞，其特
点是：胞体达30um×53um，核占优势，圆形或椭圆形，染色质疏松呈粗点网状。有1~5个灰色或灰蓝色核
仁，大者可达10um×15umm。胞浆淡蓝或略深，量少，外形极不规则，有时轮廓不清，呈撕裂状。偶尔巨大网
状细胞数目可多于巨大原始红细胞，易见退化型。
Acute Hemopoietic Arrest
Acute hemopoietic arrest is also termed as acute pure red cell aplasia,acute erythroblastopenia,
acquired acute erythropoietic hypoplasia,aplastic crisis and so on.
Bonemarrowshowserythroidaplasiaandgiantproerythroblasts.Somecasesnotonlypresentwithpure
red cell aplasia but also have the involvementof granulocytic and megakaryocyticlineages.
Hemogram Hemoglobin is (25~110)g/L,and less than 50g/L in half of cases.Reticulocytes are
decreased or even absent. The total leukocyte count isnormal,decreased or elevated with therange of
0.9x10/Lto16.2×10/L,and the differentialcountisnormalor revealsoccasionalincrease of
lymphocytes.Sometimesthe totalleukocytecountis decreased to0.4×10°/Lwithdecreasedorabsent
neutrophils.Plateletsareusually normal or decreased innumber.Reticulocytes areincreasedduring the
Neutrophilalkaline phosphatase(NAP)isusuallynormal.
MyelogramThe marrow is usuallycellular witha profound erythroid extreme hypoplasia,and an
relatively high G/E ratio.Erythroblasts may be zeroin counting 500nucleated cells.Megakaryocytes are
varyingin number.
Findinggiantproerythroblasts in thetailormarginofmarrowfilmsisoneofthemarkersofacute
hemopoietic arrest.Morethan90%caseswithacutehemopoietic arresthavegiantproerythroblasts.They
areround,ellipticor irregular in shape.Thecells are from 18um×22um to34μmx36um.Dark blue

cytoplasm maycontain somevacuolesandafewazurophilicgranules.Thenuclei areroundorelliptic
withfine spot-reticular chromatin.Sometimes thepurplish-redchromatin is coarser than thatofnormal
proerythroblasts.The nucleoli are often giant or blurry,casually withvacuoles.Moreover,mitotic figures
in diakinesis of giant proerythroblasts,polynucleatedgiant proerythroblasts and abnormal mitotic cells
can be seen.PAs staining of giant proerythroblasts is usually negative and occasionally positive.

giant proerythroblasts in number,and the degenerative reticulum cells can be seen.

再生障碍性贫血
再生障碍性贫血（Aplasticanemia，AA）是由于多种病因所致的骨髓造血组织明显减少，代之以脂肪组织，
导致外周血红细胞、白细胞和血小板明显减少即全血细胞减少。临床上以贫血、出血、感染为其特点。
血象红细胞、白细胞和血小板均减少，红细胞形态大致正常。网织红细胞也减少。白细胞分类淋巴细胞相
对增高。血小板形态不规则，小型血小板增多。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分增高。
骨髓象有核细胞增生减低或重度减低，三系造血细胞明显减少。粒、红两系多为中、晚幼阶段细胞。巨核
细胞减少或阙如。淋巴细胞、浆细胞、组织嗜碱细胞、网状细胞及脂肪细胞增多。可见非造血细胞团，但并非本
病所特有。倘若有核细胞增生活跃，巨核细胞必须明显减少，并且至少有一个部位增生不良。
Aplastic Anemia
Aplasticanemia(AA)isa clinical syndrome characterized by anemia,bleeding and infection,in
which there is a deficiency of red cells,neutrophils and platelets （pancytopenia)resulted from a failure
39
图谐
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
ofbloodcellproductionin themarrowandfattyreplacement.
HemogramThe patientswith aplasticanemia havevarying degrees of pancytopenia.Anemia is
associatedwith nomorphologicchangesandalowreticulocyteindex.The differential cell count reveals
amarked decrease inneutrophils andarelative increase inlymphocytes.Irregularplateletsmaybe seen
and small plateletsare increased.Neutrophil alkaline phosphatase(NAP)isincreased.
MyelogramHypocellular orextremelyhypocellularmarrowcontainsa fewhematopoieticcells.
Most of granulocytic and erythroid cells arein the intermediate and late stages of differentiations.
Megakaryocytes arereduced or absent.Lymphocytes,plasma cells,tissue basophils,reticulum cells and fat
cells may be predominate.Non-hematopoietic cell groups can be seen,which isnot specificfor the
disease.On occasion,ifthe marrowiscellular or evenhypercellular,thenumber ofmegakaryocytesmust
besignificantlyreducedand atleastone area of themarrowishypocellular.

慢性获得性纯红细胞再生障碍性贫血
本病特点：多见于40岁以上成人，临床上以贫血为主，骨髓中单纯红系增生不良。原发性获得性纯红细胞
再生障碍性贫血多并发胸腺瘤，部分病人免疫球蛋白异常，可能与自身免疫有关。继发性者与某些药物（如氯霉
素、磺胺、苯妥英钠等）和感染有关。贫血的症状和体征是本病的唯一表现，无发热、出血和肝脾肿大。
血象血红蛋白降低，红细胞形态正常，呈正细胞正色素性贫血。网织红细胞小于0.1%，绝对值减少。白
细胞和血小板一般正常。
但红系形态正常。粒系百分比相对升高，嗜酸性粒细胞可增多。巨核系增生正常，极少数病人巨核细胞可增多。
Chronic acquired pure red cell aplasia
Chronic acquired pure red cell aplasia (PRCA)isa disorder characterized by absence or marked
decrease in red cell production,occurringmostly in the adults older than 40years old.Many patients
41
图谱
用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
with chronicacquiredpureredcellaplasia are complicatedwiththymoma.Somepatientshaveabnormal
aplasia is associated with some medications(such as chloromycin,sulfasulfonamide and diphentoin,etc)
andinfections.Palloris usually theonly clinicalfeature without fever,bleeding andhepatosplenomegaly.
HemogramThe anemia accompanying this disease isnormochromicand normocytic,and associated
with absolutereticulocytopenia.Reticulocytecountisless than 0.1%.Leukocytes andplatelets areusually
normal.
MyelogramMarrow is cellular.It is the only characteristic that erythroid cells in different stages
are markedly reduced(erythroblast<3%~5%)withnormalmorphmous or even absent.Granulocyticcells
arerelatively increased,and there may be an increase in eosinophils.Megakaryocyte count isnormal,or
increased in few patients.

粒细胞缺乏症
成人外周血中性粒细胞严重减少，其绝对值低于0.5×10/L时，称粒细胞缺乏症（Agranulocytosis）。
临床表现为起病急骤，有畏寒或寒战、高热、头痛及周身倦怠等。最常见的是咽峡炎、扁桃体红肿、口咽部
黏膜呈现坏死性溃疡，重者肛门、阴道皆出现坏死性溃疡。容易并发伪膜性肠炎、脓毒败血症而死亡。
血象外周血白细胞总数一般小于2.0×10°/L，甚至可低于1.0×10/L。中性粒细胞常在5%~10%以下
或完全阙如，粒细胞胞浆中常有中毒颗粒和空泡变性等。淋巴细胞相对增多。红细胞或血小板计数正常。恢复期
白细胞可一过性增高，并可出现大量幼稚细胞，呈类白血病反应血象，但不久即完全恢复正常。
骨髓象可有以下三种方式：1.有核细胞增生活跃，粒细胞系统成熟障碍，仅有原始和早幼粒细胞，常
以后者为主，可有中毒颗粒和空泡变性等；2.严重病例粒系明显减少或阙如；3.有时可出现有核细胞增生
低下，浆细胞、淋巴细胞、网状细胞增多，浆细胞可高达30%～50%或更多，易见巨核细胞和粒系及红系的早
期细胞，借此可与再生障碍性贫血的骨髓象鉴别。
Agranulocytosis
Agranulocytosis means severe neutropenia,i.e,an absolute blood neutrophil countis less than 0.5x
10°/L.The patients have an acute onset and present with algor,high fever,headache and fatigue.The
most frequentmanifestations include angina,red swelling of tonsil,necroticulcer in themucousmembrane
of oral cavity,even anus and vagina in severe cases. The patients will die because of being easily
Hemogram WBCcount is usually less than 2.0×10°/L,even less than 1.0x10/L. Granulocytes
arecommonlyless than5%~10%orcompletelyabsentin seriouscases.Thecytoplasmofgranulocytes
oftenhas toxicparticles or vacuolar degeneration.Lymphocytes increase relatively.The counts of RBC
and PLT are normal.During the recovery period WBC count can elevate temporarily with a lot of
immature granulocytes,which is same to leukemoid reaction,but it gets normal very soon.
MyelogramThree phenotypes exist as followings.1. The patients have a hypercellular bone
marrowwith dysmaturity of granulocytic cells.Only myeloblasts andpredominatepromyelocytes are left,
and contains some toxicparticles or vacuolar degeneration.2.Granulocytes arefew or absentin severe
cases.3.Some patients have a hypocellular bone marrowwith increased plasma cells,lymphocytes and
reticular cells.Plasma cells are 30%~50%or even much more.The disease canbe differentiated with
aplastic anemia by the presence of megakaryocytes andmyeloid and erythroid precursor cells.

特发性血小板减少性紫癜
特发性血小板减少性紫癜（Idiopathicthrombocytopenicpurpura，ITP）属免疫性疾病，由于抗血小板
自身抗体的产生抑制骨髓巨核细胞成熟并使血小板破坏增多而导致皮肤黏膜出血，故又称为自身免疫性血小板
减少性紫癜。急性型以儿童为多见，出血程度较重，血小板显著减少。慢性型多见于青、中年妇女，主要症状是
皮肤黏膜出血，通常见于四肢，尤其以下肢多见，可同时伴有鼻出血、齿龈出血，重者口腔黏膜有血泡。若出血
过多，可出现失血性贫血。慢性型脾脏常可轻度肿大。
血象血小板计数减少，介于（30~80）×10/L之间，急性型常小于20×10/L，其形态大致正常，偶
见体积增大、颗粒减少的巨大蓝色血小板。红细胞和血红蛋白大多正常，若有贫血，其程度与出血轻重相平行。
白细胞总数一般正常，急性型可见嗜酸性粒细胞和淋巴细胞百分比略增高。
骨髓象巨核细胞增生活跃，数量正常或增多，但有成熟障碍（即左移）现象。急、慢性ITP时巨核细胞数
量及形态比较见表2。

Idiopathic thrombocytopenicpurpura
Idiopathic thrombocytopenic purpura(ITP)is an autoimmune disorder,presentswith cutanomucous
bleeding.Because autologus antiplatelet antibodies inhibit thematuration ofmegakaryocytesinbone
marrow andmeanwhileincrease the destruction ofplatelets,it is also named autoimmune thrombocy-
topenicpurpura.Acute type of this disorder occurs commonlyin children,inwhich bleeding symptom
is severe with extreme thrombocytopenia.Chronic type mostly happens in the young and middle aged
females with main manifestation of bleeding in skin and mucosa.Hemorrahage usually occurs in
extremities,especially lower extremitieswithepistaxis and gingival bleeding.Hemorrhagicbullae may
occur in oralmucosa when severe thrombocytopenia is present.The patients do notpresent with anemia
unless significant blood loss occurs.Some chronicpatientsmay have a slightly enlarged spleen.
Hemogram The count of platelets decreases,mostly between 30x10°/L and 80x10°/L,but it is
usually less than 20x10°/Lin acute type.Platelets are normal in shape.Giant blueplateletswith
decreased particles appear in rare cases.The patients usually have normal RBCand HGB.If there is an
anemia,the extentof anemia should be paralleled with the degree of blood loss.Total number of WBC
isnormal,but some acute type patients have increasedpercentages ofeosinophils and lymphocytes.
MyelogramThemarrow reveals megakaryocytichyperplasia.Megakaryocytes are normal or in-
creased in number with dysmaturation (shifting to younger and immature megakaryocytes).

嗜酸性粒细胞增多症
外周血嗜酸性粒细胞计数大于0.45×10/L时，即称为嗜酸性粒细胞增多症（Eosinophilia）。它是由多种
病因引起的综合征，以寄生虫感染最常见。临床上所谓“高嗜酸性粒细胞增多综合征”（hypereosinophilic
syndrome）是指一组嗜酸性粒细胞显著增多，其绝对值持续大于1.5×10°/L半年以上，且极少有幼稚细胞，同
时伴有多脏器浸润（如肝脾和淋巴结肿大）的嗜酸性粒细胞增多性疾病的总称。
血象白细胞总数常增高，分类时嗜酸性粒细胞明显增多，占20%左右，亦可高达80%以上，绝对值常大
于0.6×10/L，均为成熟的嗜酸性粒细胞。血小板正常。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃或明显活跃，嗜酸性粒细胞明显增多，可高达50%以上，以成熟型为主，并可
见较多啫酸性中幼、晚幼粒细胞。红系及巨核系细胞正常。
Eosinophilia
Eosinophilia refers that the absolute count of eosinophils is higher than 0.45x10°/L.It is a
syndrome caused by many reasons in which the most common is parasite infections. The striking
eosinophilia usually with a count of eosinophils greater than 1.5x10/L over halfyear,and few blastic
cells and aninfiltration of multiple organs (such as hepatosplenomegaly and lymphnodeenlargement)was
clinically identified as hypereosinophilic syndrome.
HemogramThe key finding is a leukocytosis with a striking eosinophilia.Eosinophil count is
usually about 20 percent of white blood cells,evenup to80% ormore in severe cases,with its absolute
number often higher than 0.6x10°/L.However, they are all mature cells.Platelets are usually normal.
MyelogramThepatientshaveahypercellularbonemarrowwithmarkedlyincreasedproportion of
eosinophils,even up to more than 50%.Mature eosinophils are predominant,but a lot of eosinophilic
myelocytes andmetamyelocytes also appear.Erythropoiesis andmegakaryocytopoiesis arenormal.

Endothelial cells appear in theperipheral blood ofpatients with subacute bacterial endocarditis or
septicemia,andrarely healthy persons.

类白血病反应
类白血病反应（Leukemoidreaction）是由于某些因素（如感染、恶性肿瘤、急性中毒、急性溶血、急性
大失血等）所激发的类似白血病的血象反应。表现为外周血白细胞总数增高，常大于50×10/L，或血象中出现
幼稚型细胞，去除原发病后血象改变即可恢复正常。根据反应细胞类型不同，临床上分为中性粒细胞型、单核细
胞型、淋巴细胞型、嗜酸粒细胞型类白血病反应，但以中性粒细胞型最为常见，其血象和骨髓象如下。
血象白细胞总数大多升高，可达（50~100）×10/L或更高，也可正常或减低。分类时，中性粒细胞明
显增多，易见中毒颗粒或空泡，杆状核粒细胞比值增高呈核左移，并出现晚幼粒、中幼粒甚或早幼粒乃至原始粒
细胞，但原幼粒小于10%，偶有高达50%者。多数病人NAP积分增高，红细胞、血红蛋白和血小板正常。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃或明显活跃，以粒系增生为主，常见核左移并有中毒颗粒和空泡变性。红系与巨
核系多无明显改变。
Leukemoid reaction
Leukemoid reaction refers toa blood reaction stimulated by some factors(such as infections,
malignant tumors,acute poisoning,acute hemolysis or acute blood loss and so on)and is similar to
leukemia.It is characterized by the increased count of WBC,usually over 50x10/L,or the presence of
blasts in peripheral blood.This abnormal change will disappear with the cure of original disorders.
According to the kind of reactive cells,it is divided into four types,i.e,neutrophilic,monocytic,
lymphocytic and eosinophilic types.Among these types,neutrophilic type is the most common.
HemogramThe total count of WBC usually increases,even up to (50~100)x10°/L.It can also
decrease or do not change much in some cases.The diffenrential count shows a markedly increased
proportion of neutrophils with toxic particles orvacuoles sometimes.The proportion of stabcells rises,
whichis calledaleft-shift ofnuclei,with the presence ofmetamyelocytes,myelocytes,promyelocytes and
even myeloblasts.However,a totalproportion of myeloblasts andpromyelocytes is less than 10%.Inrare
cases,it is over 50%. Most patients have an increased score of NAP. RBC,HGB and PLT usually are
normal.
MyelogramThepatientshave a hypercelularbonemarrowwithmarkedlypredominantmyelopoiesis,
a left-shift of nuclei and toxicparticles andvacuolar degeneration of granulocytes.Erythropoiesis and
megakaryocytopoiesis are normal.

传染性单核细胞增多症
传染性单核细胞增多症（Infectiousmononucleosis）是由Epstein-Barr（EB）病毒感染B淋巴细胞引起T
淋巴细胞反应，导致自限性淋巴系统增生性疾病。临床上以发热、咽峡炎、淋巴结肿大、肝脾肿大、血中淋巴细
胞增多和出现异型淋巴细胞、血清中可检出嗜异凝集素及抗EB病毒抗体为特征。本病为散发性，秋冬季多见。
血象红细胞与血小板一般正常。患病初期白细胞可低于正常或正常，以后渐增，多数在（10~30）×10/L
之间。分类中淋巴细胞增多，并出现异型淋巴细胞（Downey细胞），可占20%~50%。个别患者可有粒细胞缺乏。
异型淋巴细胞亦可见于其他病毒性疾病，如流行性出血热（此时，尚有血小板减少和幼稚细胞）、病毒性肝炎、麻
疹和腮腺炎等。异型淋巴细胞分为三型。
骨髓象无明显改变，异型淋巴细胞数量明显少于血象。
Infectious mononucleosis
Infectious mononucleosis is defined as a self-limited lymphoproliferative disease which is caused by
51

EBvirus(EBV).EBV infects B lymphocytes so thatan immuneresponse fromT lymphocytesiselicited
Clinically it is characterized by fever,angina,enlargement oflymph nodes,liver and spleen,increased
lymphocytesand atypical lymphocytesin theblood,heterophileagglutininand EBVantibodiesin the
sera.The disease is sporadicandmostlyhappensin autumn andwinter.
HemogramRBCandPLT arecommonly normal.The countofWBCdecreases or changeslessin
theearly stage,but increases with the progression of the disease,usually up to（10~30)x 10/L.The
proportion of lymphocytes rises,and atypical lymphocytes (Downey cells) appear which can occupy
20%~50%ofWBC.Agranulocytosisoccursinfewcases.Atypical lymphocytesalsopresent in other
diseases,such as epidemic hemorrhagic fever(with thrombocytopenia and blasts),viral hepatitis,measles
andmumps.There arethreetypesofatypicallymphocytes.
MyelogramThe bone marrow has not obvious changes.Atypical lymphocytes are significantly
fewer than thatintheperipheralblood.

陪格尔（Pelger）白细胞形态异常
本病的主要临床表现为遗传性中性粒细胞分叶过少，但其吞噬功能正常，故不影响病人健康。
血象白细胞不增多。红细胞和血小板正常。可见Pelger细胞。
骨髓象骨髓有核细胞增生正常，主要可见Pelger细胞。其形态特点：核不分叶，呈花生形、肾形、哑铃
形和圆形等，但多为未分开的两个叶，短粗，染色质密集成块。胞浆内颗粒稍大，可见中毒颗粒。
上述畸形也可见于MDS、伤寒、疤疾等，但无家族史，故称假性Pelger畸形。
Pelger-HuetAnomaly
The Pelger-Huet anomalyis an inherited disorder characterized by abnormal lobe development of
granulocytes.Neutrophils can havemonolobed or bilobed appearance with normal phagocyticfunction so
that the health of patients isnotaffected
Hemogram WBC count does not increase. RBC and PLT are normal.Pelger cells can be seen.
feature of Pelger cells is with an unseperated nucleus which can be peanut-like,reniform,dumb-bell-like
orround.Most nuclei have two short and thick lobes without separation.The chromatin aggregates in
clumps.The cytoplasm contains large granules and toxicparticles.
The malformation can also appear in MDS, typhoid and malaria,and so on,which is named as
pseudoPelger-Huetanomalybecause thereisnoinherited tendency.

Chediak-Higashi Syndrome
Chediak-Higashi Syndrome（CHS）又称先天性白细胞颗粒异常综合征，属常染色体隐性遗传，男女均可
罹患。临床特征是婴幼儿发病。皮肤白化，畏光，易被细菌和病毒感染。肝脾和淋巴结肿大。白细胞出现异常颗
粒，常有家族史。
血象和骨髓象中，白细胞含有异常颗粒，其特点为嗜酸性，呈圆形、椭圆形或不规则形，瑞氏-姬姆萨染色
呈黄红色或紫红色，直径1～7um，一至数个不等。见于早幼粒细胞以下的粒系细胞及淋巴细胞、异型淋巴细胞
和单核细胞。异常颗粒周围常有透光带。如染色不佳则呈灰色。幼红细胞内也可偶见。粒细胞及单核细胞内可见
空泡。异型淋巴细胞可增多。
Chediak-Higashi Syndrome
The Chediak-Higashi Syndrome (CHS),an autosomal recessive disease,is also named as congenital
abnormalleukocyticgranules syndrome.The disease occurs in bothmale and female.Characteristically
the patients with CHS are infants with light skin,photophobia and susceptibility to bacterial or viral
infections.Thepatients can have hepatosplenomegaly and lymph node enlargement.Abnormalgiant
granules appear in leukocytes.The patients often have a family history.
In theperipheralblood andbonemarrow,leukocytes contain abnormal granuleswhich are acidophilic
Theround or ovalgranules arered or purplish-redwithWright-Giemsa stainingand 1-7micrometers
in diameter.The number of the granules can be one or several.They canbe seenin lymphocytes,atypical
lymphocytes,monocytes and granulocytes which are more mature than promyelocytes.Around the
abnormal granules, there is usually a lucency band.And they are gray when the staining is not good.
Some vacuoles can be seen in granulocytes and monocytes.Atypical lymphocytes increase.

白血病
白血病（Leukemias）是造血系统原因未明的一组恶性疾病，其特征是在造血组织中，某一类白血病细胞无限
制地异常增生，并浸润到各组织器官特别是肝脾和淋巴结。在外周血中常有幼稚细胞出现。
根据病情急缓和细胞分化程度分为：①急性白血病：起病急剧，以发热、贫血、出血为主要表现，骨髓
及外周血象中以异常的原始和幼稚细胞为主；②慢性白血病：经过缓慢，病程较长，症状轻微，常因其他疾
病就诊或查体时脾脏肿大被发现。骨髓及外周血中以异常的成熟细胞为主，其次是幼稚细胞，原始细胞较少。
根据白血病细胞类型不同又分为淋巴细胞白血病和非淋巴细胞白血病。
急性淋巴细胞白血病
根据1980年9月28日在苏州市召开的全国白血病分类分型经验交流讨论会，对急性淋巴细胞白血病分型标
准提出以下建议。
第一型（L型）：原始和幼稚细胞以小细胞（直径<12um）为主；核圆形，偶有凹陷或折叠，染色质较粗，结
55
图谐
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOG
构较一致，核仁小而少，不清楚；胞浆少，轻或中度嗜碱。过氧化物酶或苏丹黑染色阳性的原始细胞一般不超过3%。
第二型（L型）：原始和幼稚细胞以大细胞（直径可大于正常小淋巴细胞的2倍以上，>12um）为主；核
形不规则，凹陷和折叠可见。染色质疏松，结构较不一致，核仁较清楚，一或多个；胞浆量常较多，轻或中度啫
碱，有些细胞深染
第三型（L型）：似Burkit型，原始和幼稚细胞大小较为一致。以大细胞为主；核形较规则。染色质呈均
匀细点状，核仁明显，一或多个，呈小泡状；胞浆量较多，深蓝色，空泡常明显，呈蜂窝状。
急性淋巴细胞白血病三种亚型的形态特点（见表3）。

Leukemias
Leukemias are a heterogeneous group of malignant hematopoietic disorders of unknown origin.They
arecharacterized by immortalproliferation ofonekindofblasts inhematopoietictissue,which infiltrate
various tissues and organs especially liver,spleen and lymph nodes. There is usually the presence of blasts
or immaturecellsin theperipheralblood.
Leukemias are divided intoacute and chronic typesaccording to the onset andmature extentof
blasts.① Acute leukemias(AL):Patients have an acute onset with the main manifestations of fever,
anemia and bleeding.Thepredominantcells inthebonemarrowandperipheralblood areabnormalblasts
and immature cells. Chronic leukemias The diseases progress slowly with a long course and slight
symptoms.Patients are often diagnosed accidentallybecauseof splenomegaly on routine medical exami-
nation or consulting a doctor for other diseases.The predominant cells in the bone marrow and
peripheral blood are abnormal mature cells, and then immature cells with fewblasts.
Leukemias also are divided into lymphoid and myeloid (or nonlymphocytic）types according to the
morphologyofblastcells.
Acute lymphocytic leukemia (ALL)
Ltype:predominant small blasts and immature cells（diameter<12μm),round nuclei with introcessions
and foldings,coarse chromatin withhomogenous structure,small andindistinctor absentnucleoli,scanty
cytoplasm with mild or moderate basophilla.The blasts which are positive in POX and Sudan black
staining are often less than3%.
Ltype:predominant large blasts and immature cells(diameter>12μm),irregular nuclei,loose
chromatin with heterogenous structures,clear one or several nucleoli,more cytoplasm with mild or
moderate basophilla,deeply stained in some cells.
Ltype:predominant large blasts and immature cells similar to Burkitt cells,homogenous fine spot
chromatin,regular nuclei,theprominent nucleoli which arevesicles shaped,abundant darkblue cyto-
plasmwithobviousvecuoles andhoneycombappearance.

急性非淋巴细胞白血病
1986年9月20日在天津召开的白血病分类、分型讨论会上，对急性非淋巴细胞白血病（简称急非淋，ANLL）
分型提出以下诊断标准（略有增补）。
（一）原粒细胞的形态分为两型
I型—典型原粒细胞，胞浆中无颗粒。
Ⅱ型
一有原粒细胞的特征，胞浆量较少，有少量颗粒。
原始单核细胞的形态也分I、Ⅱ两型，标准同原粒细胞。
（二）急性非淋巴细胞白血病分型
1.急性粒细胞白血病未分化型（M）
骨髓中原粒细胞（1型+Ⅱ型）≥90%（非红系细胞），早幼粒细胞很少，中性中幼粒细胞以下阶段不见或
罕见。
2.急性粒细胞白血病部分分化型（M）
分为以下两种亚型：
M：骨髓中原粒细胞为（1+Ⅱ型）为30%~90%（非红系细胞），单核细胞<20%，早幼粒细胞以下阶
段的细胞>10%
M2：骨髓中原始及早幼粒细胞明显增多，以异常的中性中幼粒细胞增生为主，其胞核常有核仁，有明
显的核浆发育不平衡，此类细胞>30%。
3.急性颗粒增多的早幼粒细胞白血病（M）
骨髓中以颗粒增多的异常早幼粒细胞增生为主，>30%（非红系细胞），其胞核大小不一，胞浆中有大小不
等的颗粒。患者白血病细胞中存在染色体易位t（15;17）和/或PML/RARα融合基因。
可分为三种亚型：
（1）M（粗颗粒型）嗜苯胺蓝颗粒粗大，密集甚至融合。
（2）M（细颗粒型）嗜苯胺蓝颗粒密集而细小。
（3）M（变异型）嗜苯胺蓝颗粒微小，分散，光镜下不易识别，需染色体或融合基因检测加以诊断。
4.急性粒-单核细胞白血病（M）
按粒系和单核细胞系形态不同，可分为以下四种类型：
（1）M4以原始和早幼粒细胞增生为主，原、幼单核细胞和单核细胞》20%（非红系细胞）。
（2）M4以原、幼单核细胞增生为主，原始和早幼粒细胞>20%（非红系细胞）。
（3）M以原始细胞既具粒细胞系又具单核细胞系形态特征者>30%（非红系细胞）。
60
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
（4）M4以除上述特点外，含有粗大而圆的嗜酸颗粒及着色较深的嗜碱颗粒的嗜酸粒细胞，占5%-30%（非
红系细胞）。
5.急性单核细胞白血病（M）
分以下两种亚型。
（1）未分化型（Msa）骨髓中原始单核细胞（I型+Ⅱ型）》80%（非红系细胞）。
（2）部分分化型（M）骨髓中原始和幼稚单核细胞>30%（非红系细胞）；原始单核细胞（1型+Ⅱ型）
<80%（非红系细胞）
6.红白血病（M）
骨髓中红细胞系>50%，且带有形态学异常，骨髓非红细胞系原粒细胞（或原始+幼稚单核细胞）1型+Ⅱ
型>30%。若血片中原粒细胞或原始单核细胞>5%，骨髓非红系细胞中原粒细胞或原始+幼稚单核细胞>20%。
7.巨核细胞白血病（M）
（1）未分化型外周血中有原巨核（小巨核）细胞；骨髓中原巨核细胞≥30%：原巨核细胞有电镜或单克
隆抗体证实；骨髓细胞少，往往干抽，活检有原始细胞和巨核细胞增多，网状纤维增加。
（2）分化型骨髓及外周血中以单圆核和多圆核病态巨核细胞为主。
急性白血病的临床表现发病急，进展快，常有贫血、出血、感染。罹患本病时各器官和组织均有不同程度
的细胞浸润，如肝脾和淋巴结肿大，尤其急淋病人较多见。可有骨关节疼痛，胸骨压痛具有一定的诊断意义。偶
尔骨膜上出现无痛性肿块，最多发生于眼眶周围，也可出现在颅骨、胸骨、肋骨或四肢骨，称为绿色瘤，多见于
急粒病人。齿龈增生和肿胀常见于急性单核细胞白血病。无痛性睾丸肿大多发生于急淋治疗后的病人，活检时常
常显示有白血病细胞浸润。累及神经系统时，称中枢神经系统白血病（CNSL），以急淋最多见。表现为颅内压增
高的症状和体征，脑脊液压力增高，超过0.02kPa（200mm水柱）。脑脊液内：①白细胞数>0.01×10/L；②
涂片可找到白血病细胞；③蛋白>450mg/L或潘氏试验阳性
血象红细胞和血红蛋白均有不同程度的减少，一般为正细胞正色素性贫血。网织红细胞正常或减少，偶可
高于正常，但不超过5%。外周血可见幼红细胞。近半数病例白细胞总数在10×10/L以下，白血性白血病时可
高达（20~50）×10/L或更高，非白血性白血病时常在（1.0~3.0）×10/L或更低，分类中可见原始和幼稚
细胞。血小板一般均减少，出血时间延长，束臂试验常呈阳性，血块退缩不良。
骨髓象骨髓检查是诊断急性白血病最主要的依据。其主要所见是：①有核细胞增生明显或极度活跃；②
某一类型的白血病细胞增生，并以原、幼阶段细胞为主，约占30%~99%；③原幼细胞恶性变明显；④在急性粒
和急性单核白血病时，胞浆中有时可见棒状小体（Auer小体）。细胞化学染色可确定白血病类型（见表4）。
急性白血病MIC分型：以上介绍FAB分型，在白血病分型上起到重要作用。但不足之处是重复性不高，有
一定的主观性。故1986年扩大的FAB协作组提出了形态学（Morphology，M）、免疫学（Immunology，I）、细
胞遗传学（Cytogenetics，C）MIC三方面检查使白血病的分型准确率明显提高。

Acute nonlymphocytic leukemia(ANLL)
1.There are two types of myeloblasts.
TypeI:typicalmyeloblastswithoutgranulesin thecytoplasm
TypeIl:havingthefeaturesofmyeloblatswithlesscytoplasmandafewgranules.
61
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
Monoblasts also are divided into two types (type I+ type Il) according to the above criteria.
2.Types ofANLL
①Acutemyelocyticleukemia(AML)withoutmaturation（FABM)
Blasts (I+Il) in bone marrow have a proportion equal to or over 90% of nonerythroid cells with
few promyelocytes.Myelocytes and othermore mature granulocytes are absent or rare.
②AMLwith partial maturation（FABM)
Itis dividedinto two subtypes.
M:Blasts (I+) in bone marrow have aproportion from 30%to 90%of non erythroid cells.
Monocytesare less than 20%.More mature myelocytic cells than promyelocytesconsistofat least 10%of
nonerythroid cells.
M:Besides increasedmyeloblasts and promyelocytes,abnormalneutrophilicmyelocytes are predominant.
These myelocytes have obviousnucleoli andmaturation asynchrony between nuclei and cytoptasma,
whichcomposeofatleast30%ofnonerythroidcells.
③Acutepromyelocyticleukemia（APL)(FABM)
Abnormal promyelocyteswith increasedgranules are predominant in bonemarrow,which compose
ofover3o%ofnonerythroidcells.Theyhave variablysizednucleiandgranulesin the cytoplasm.The
patientswith APL have the chromosome t（15;17) and/or PML/RARa gene.APL is dividedinto three
types:
M(Coarse granular type):Azurophillic granules are large,dense and even in fusion.
Ms(Fine granular type):Azurophillic granules are fine and dense.
M(Microgranular type）:Micro azurophillicgranules arelessprominent,somewhat dispersed,and
may be difficult tovisualize using lightmicroscopy.The diagnosis is often made by finding the typical
chromosome t(15;17)or PML/RARαgene.
④Acute myelomonocyticleukemia(FAB M)
It is divided into four subtypes according to the morphous ofmyeloid and monocytic cellsin bone
marrow.
Ma:Myeloblasts and promyelocytes are predominant.Monoblasts andpromonocytes andmonocytes
compose of at least 20%of nonerythroid cells.
Mas:Monoblasts andpromonocytes are predominant.Myeloblasts andpromyelocytes compose of at
least20%ofnonerythroidcells
30%ofnonerythroid cells.
M:Besides the above characteristics the eosinophils with coarse,round and acidophil granules and
deeply stainedbasophilic granules composeof5%~30%ofnonerythroid cells.
Acute monocyticleukemia(FAB M)
Itis divided into two subtypes.
Ms(Undifferentiated type):Monoblasts （type I+ type II) compose of at least 80%of nonerythroid
cells in bone marrow.
Ms,(Partial differentiated type):Monoblasts andpromonocytes compose of at least30%ofnonerythroid
cells in bonemarrow.Monoblasts(typeI+ type I)areless than 80%
Erythroleukemia(FABM)
Erythroid cellswith morphologic abnormalities are more than50%of bonemarrow cells.Myeloblasts
marrow.If myeloblasts or monoblasts aremore than5%inperipheralblood,myeloblasts or monoblasts
andpromonocytes should be more than 20%of nonerythroid cells inbone marrow.
①Megakaryocyticleukemia(FAB M)
62
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOG
Undifferentiated type:Megakaryoblasts(micromegakaryocytes)appearintheperipheralblood.They
compose of at least30%ofbonemarrow cells and areidentified by electron microscope or monoclonal
antibodies.Bone marrowaspiration often showsadry tapwhenhematopoieticcellsarenotmany.The
Differentiated type:Abnormal megakaryocytes with single and multiple round nuclei are predomi-
nantinthebonemarrowandperipheralblood.
Clinical manifestatiosofacute leukemias The patients with AL have an acute onset and rapid
progression with the symptoms of anemia,bleeding and infection.When thepatients go to see a doctor,
they usually have blast infiltration in tissues and organs,such as liver,spleen and lymph nodes,which
ismore common in acute lymphocytic leukemia.Bone orjointpain may appear in some patients and a
sternal tenderness is meaningful to the diagnosis.Some patientswith acute myelocyticleukemia(AML)
have chloroma,which refers to the painless lumps in the periosteum,occuring mostly in periorbital area
and also in cranium,sternum,ribs and limb bones.The patients with acute monocyticleukemia often
complain of gum hypertrophy and swelling.Painless intumescence of testismostly happens in ALL
patients after treatment,the biopsy of which shows leukemic cell infiltration. Centralneural system
leukemia (CNSL）refers to the blast infiltration of central neural system,which mostly occurs in ALL
patients with the symptoms and signs ofcranial hypertension.The CsF tension increases over 0.o2kPa
(200mm HO).CSF examination reveals WBC>0.01×10/L,blasts in the smear and protein>450mg/Lor
Pan test positive.
Hemogram RBC and HGB decrease in various degrees. Anemia is usually normocellular and
normochromatic.The count of reticulocytes isnormal or decreases,occasionly increases but less than 5%.
Erythroblastsmayappearin theperipheral blood of somepatients.Nearly halfof thepatientspresents
with a WBCcount lower than 10×10/L.It can behighereven up to(20~50)x10°/L or much more
in leukemicleukemias.In nonleukemicleukemias,thepatientspresent with aWBCcountbetween（1.0~
3.0)x1o/Lormuch lower.The differential countofWBCpresents blasts and immature cells.PLT count
usually decreases.Bleeding time prolongs and cuff test is positive.Clot retraction is abnormal.
MyelogramBone marrowexamination gives the most importantevidence to diagnoseleukemias.
Themainfindingsinclude ①hypercellular;proliferationofleukemiccellswith thepredominance of
blasts andimmature cellsup to 30%~99%;③obviously malignant change of blasts and immature cells;
leukemias. Cytochemistry staining is helpful to determine the typesof leukemias.
The MIC classification of acute leukemia:The FAB classification of leukemias described above has
play an importantrole inthe classification ofleukemia.However,the FAB classification is also limited
by the lower repeatability and the subjectivity.Therefore,FAB Cooperative Group hasrecommended the
MICclassification depending on the morphology (M),immunology (I) and cytogenetics (C) to increase the
accuracyof leukemiaclassification.

颗粒性淋巴细胞白血病
颗粒性淋巴细胞白血病（granularlymphocyteleukemia，GLL）属于克隆性增殖性疾病。颗粒性淋巴细
胞是指一个淋巴细胞不论其分化程度如何，含有3个以上的嗜苯胺蓝颗粒。正常人血象中的颗粒性淋巴细胞多属
于大淋巴细胞，大部分为自然杀伤（Naturalkiller，NK）细胞，部分属T细胞。正常人颗粒细胞的绝对数，男性
为（0.63±0.261）×10/L，女性为（0.35±0.176）×10/L，当其绝对值超过2.0×10/L时称为颗粒性淋巴
细胞增生性疾病（Granularlymphocyteproliferativedisease，GLPD），有原发和继发之分。颗粒性淋巴细胞
白血病多为急性，属于原发性GLPD如按FAB分型为L型或L2型。有的不是克隆性增殖性疾病，又无其他基础
疾病，称为特发性GLPD，有的继发于慢性风湿性关节炎、肿瘤及脾切除术后等。
Granular lymphocyte leukemia
Granular lymphocyte leukemia(GLL)is a clonal proliferative disorder. The so called “granular
lymphocytes”refers to the lymphocytes which havemore than three azurophilicgranulesin the
cytoplasmregardless oftheir differentiation degrees.Mostgranular lymphocytes innormalpersonsbelong
to large lymphocytes. The majority of them are natural killer (NK) cell, some are T lymphocytes. The
absolutecountinnormalmaleand femaleare（0.63±0.261）×10/Land（0.35±0.176）x10/L,
respectively.It is named granular lymphocyte proliferative disease (GLPD) that the absolute count is more
than 2.0x10/L,which is divided intoprimary or secondary type.Mostpatientswith GLL oftenhave
an acuteonset and areprimary,belongingtoLorLtype accordingtoFABclassifications.Some patients
with GLL are called idiopathic GLPD because their diseases arenotclonal and proliferative,and they
have no underlying diseases.Some patientswith secondary GLPD are caused by chronicrheumatic
arthritis,tumorsor splenectomy.
79

嗜酸性粒细胞白血病
嗜酸性粒细胞白血病（Eosinophilicleukemia）是一种罕见的白血病，其特点是血液及骨髓中有较多的幼
稚嗜酸性粒细胞。嗜酸性粒细胞浸润各脏器，尤其是心肺和中枢神经系统。临床表现除发热、出血、贫血、骨痛
和肝脾、淋巴结肿大外，尚有进行性心力衰竭、呼吸困难和中枢神经系统症状，如精神障碍、视力减退、共济失
调甚至偏瘫等。
血象白细胞总数常明显增高，可达（50~200）×10/L，嗜酸性粒细胞常占60%以上，可高达90%，并
可见幼稚啫酸性粒细胞。血红蛋白和血小板均可减少。
骨髓象嗜酸性粒细胞从早幼到成熟各阶段均增生，呈核左移。有较多幼稚嗜酸性粒细胞，胞体大小不
，胞浆淡蓝，嗜酸性颗粒粗大，分布不匀，有时有空泡，尚可含有多少不等的嗜碱性颗粒。部分嗜酸性中
幼粒细胞可见1～2个核仁。原始粒细胞大于5%。
Eosinophili leukemia
Eosinophilic leukemia is a rare type of leukemias.It is characterized by the presence of immature
eosinophiliccellsintheperipheralbloodandbonemarrow.Abnormaleosinophiliccellsinfiltrateinto
many organsespecially heart,lungs and central nervous system.The clinical manifestations include fever,
bleeding,anemia,bone pain,hepatosplenomegaly and lymphnode enlargement,and alsoprogressive heart
failure,dyspnea,and CNS symptoms such as mental dysfunction,visional retardation,ataxia and
hemiparalysis.
Hemogram wBC count remarkably increases,even up to （50~200)x10/L.The proportion of
eosinophilic cells is often above 60%,even up to 90%.And immature cosinophilic cells can be seen.Both
HGB and PLT may be reduced.
Myelogram Eosinophilic cell hyperplasia exists in all stages from promyelocytes to mature cells,
which presents a left-shift ofnuclei.A lot ofimmature eosinophilic cells can be seen.They are different
in size.The blue cytoplasm contains some scattering coarse eosinophilic granuleswith vacuoles and some
basophilic granules sometimes. Some eosinophilic myelocytes have 1~2 nucleoli.The proportion of
myeloblasts is over5%.

嗜碱性粒细胞白血病
嗜碱性粒细胞白血病（Basophilicleukemia）是一种罕见的白血病，各年龄组均可发病。典型病例有重度
贫血、发热、出血和肝脾肿大，但淋巴结肿大较少见。
血象白细胞总数大多升高，偶尔高达50×10/L，但也可低至1.1×10°/L。分类时嗜碱性粒细胞明显增
多，常大于60%，可高达100%，并出现较多的幼稚型嗜碱性粒细胞。血红蛋白与血小板均常减少。可见幼红细
胞。
骨髓象可见大量嗜碱性粒细胞。嗜碱性早幼、中幼和晚幼粒细胞增多，嗜碱性颗粒粗大、稠密，可部分或
全部遮住胞浆和/或胞核
嗜碱性细胞用甲苯胺蓝（或闪光蓝Astiablue）染色时呈阳性反应。
Basophilic leukemia
Basophilic leukemia is a rare disease.It occurs in the patients in different age groups.It is
characterized by severe anemia,fever,bleeding and hepatosplenomegaly.However,lymphadenopathy is
not common.
HemogramThe WBC count mostly increases andcan reach 50x10/Lin fewcases.It can also
be reduced to 1.1x10/L in somepatients.The differential count reveals markedbasophilia.Basophilic
granulocytes are often more than 60%,evenup to100%of totalwBCwith a lot ofimmature cells.The
levelsofHGBandPLTusuallydecrease.Immatureerythrocytescan beseen.
MyleogramA large number of basophils can be found.Basophilicpromyelocytes,myelocytes and
metamyelocytes are increased.Basophilicgranules are coarse and condensedwhich cover the cytoplasm
and/or nucleoli partly or entirely.In toluidine blue (or Astia blue) staining,basophilic cells give a
positive reaction.

全髓白血病
全髓白血病（Panmyelosis）是骨髓中红、白及巨核三系细胞同时异常增生的一种急性非淋巴细胞白血病，亦
称红白巨血病。男女均可发病，临床表现为进行性贫血、出血、反复感染及脏器浸润。约半数病例肝脾、淋巴结
肿大，常有胸骨压痛。
血象血红蛋白降低，血小板大多减少，且伴有形态异常如颗粒减少的巨大血小板。可见数量不等的幼红细
胞，亦可有原粒、早幼粒和/或原、幼单核细胞。偶见Auer小体。少数病例有巨核细胞。
骨髓象有核细胞增生明显活跃或极度活跃，红、粒系及巨核细胞系均异常增生。幼红细胞有巨幼样变，并
可见多核、核分叶、核出芽等畸形，尚可出现环状铁粒幼红细胞。粒系核浆发育不平衡，核分叶过多，也可有
Pelger畸形。胞浆颗粒减少，原粒细胞中偶见Auer小体。幼巨核细胞为圆形或椭圆形，常有芽状突起，胞浆量
少，可有空泡，核呈圆形，较规则，染色质稍粗，核仁1~2个。尚可见较多的变性巨核细胞，胞体大小相差悬
殊，多数偏小，有一或多个小而圆的细胞核，可见核分叶现象。时有幼巨核细胞产血小板，胞浆量多少不一，颗
粒稀少或阙如，可有吞噬现象或空泡。
83
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
Panmyelosis
Panmyelosis refers to a non-lymphocytic leukemia which has abnormal hyperplasia of tri-lineages
(including erythrocytic,leukocytic and megakaryocytic series）.The disease has no sex dominance.Clinical
manifestations arecharacterized byprogressive anemia,bleeding,repeated infections and organ infiltration.
About half of the patients have hepatosplenomegaly and lymphadenopathy.Sternal tenderness is often
present.
HemogramHGB level is reduced and PLT count decreases inmost ofpatients with thepresence
of abnormal gaint platelets containing fewer particles.Normoblasts can be found in different numbers.
Myeloblasts,promyelocytes and/or monoblasts and promonocytes may appear.Auer rods and mega-
karyocytes can be seen in few cases.
MyelogramThepatients havehypercellular or markedlyhypercellularbone marrow.All the three
lineages have abnormal hyperplasia.Normoblasts havemegaloblastoidchangeswith somemalformations
such as polynucleation,karyolobism andnuclear budding.Ring sideroblasts can be seen.The granulocytic
lineagehas developmentasynchronyofnucleiandcytoplasm,hypersegmentednucleiandPelgermalformation.
The granules in the cytoplasm are reduced,and Auer rods may be found in some myeloblasts.
androundnucleiwith coarse chromatin mayhave1-2nucleoli.A lotof degenerated megakaryocytes
appear in quitely different sizes,most of them are small with one or several small round nuclei.
Karyolobism is present.Sometimesimmature platelet-producing megakaryocytes can be found.These cells
havevaryingamount of the cytoplasm whichcontains fewer or nogranules.Phagocytic phenomena or
vacuolesmay existin some cells.

毛细胞白血病
毛细胞白血病（Hairycellleukemia，HCL）是一种特殊类型的白血病，属慢性淋巴细胞增生性疾病。其
临床特点是起病隐袭，慢性经过，脾脏明显肿大。白细胞常增多，红细胞和血小板正常或减少。外周血与骨髓中
找到特征性的毛细胞是诊断本病的主要依据。毛细胞大多来源于B细胞，来源于T细胞者少见。
血象可呈全血细胞减少，红细胞和血小板减少较为常见。白细胞可低至3.0×10/L，但约半数病例白细
胞总数高于正常，可达20.0×10/L以上。毛细胞占30%~90%，平均大于10%。偶见幼粒和幼红细胞。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃或明显活跃，亦可“干抽”。可见较多的毛细胞，平均30%以上。其形态特点是
在光学显微镜下，大小与大淋巴细胞相似，外形为圆形或椭圆形，约13~16pm，也可大到30m。核呈圆形、椭
圆形或有凹陷，核膜清楚，染色质粗点网状，核仁可有可无。胞浆量多少不一，染灰蓝或淡蓝色，无颗粒或有少
许嗜苯胺蓝颗粒，边缘不规则，可见为数不等的绒毛状突出物，长者可达10um以上，有时绒毛基底部较宽，顶
端纤细呈伪足状。在相差显微镜下可见这种绒毛状突起物左右摆动，伸缩变形。
细胞化学染色毛细胞酸性磷酸酶染色阳性且不被酒石酸抑制；糖原染色可呈阳性；过氧化物酶和碱性磷
酸酶染色阴性；酯酶染色呈阴性或阳性。
扫描电镜可见细胞表面有较多散射的细长毛状突起，延伸的细毛有交叉现象。某些毛细胞表面呈皱褶状突
起。
透射电镜下除显示毛状突起外，细胞浆内还可看到核糖体板层复合物（PLC）。
Hairy cell leukemia
Hairy cell leukemia (HCL) is a special kind of leukemias and belongs to chronic lymphoproliferative
disorders. Clinicallyit is characterized by anindolent onset,slowprogression with massive splenomegaly.
The count of WBC often increases with normal or decreased RBC and PLT.Typical hairy cells found in
the peripheral blood and bone marrow are important evidence for diagnosis.Hairy cells are of B-cell
origin in most patients, of T-cell origin only in rare cases.
HemogramThe patients generallyhave pancytopenia.Anemia and thrombocytopenia are common.
WBC can be lower than 3x10°/L,buthalf of thepatientshave leukocytosis even higher than 20×10°/
L.30%~90%of leukocytes are hairy cells with the median over 10%.Normoblasts andimmature
granulocytes can befound occasionally.
MyelogramThepatients can have a hypercellular or dry tap bone marrow.Many hairy cells appear
in bone marrow,usually with a proportion over 30%.Their morphological characteristics under light
85
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOG
microscope are similar to large lymphocytes in size.The hairy cells are round and oval in shape,13μ
m~16μmorup to 30μm indiameter.Thenuclei are round,ovalorreniformwith a clearnuclear
membrane and coarsereticular chromatin.The nucleoli are present or not.The abundant or less
cytoplasm is gray-blue or slight blue containingno or a few azurophilic granules.The margin of the
cytoplasm is irregular with villiform projections ofwhich the longestone is over 10pm.Sometimes the
villis have abroad base and a slender tip justaspseudopods.Underphase difference microscope,the
villiform projections swingright and left change their shapes.
Cytochemistry stainingAcid phosphatase staining is positive andnotinhibited by tartaric acid for
hairy cells. Staining for glycogen is positive.Peroxydase and alkaline phosphatase stainings are negative.
Esterase staining is positive or negative.
Under scanningelectronmicroscope,there are a lot of scattering slender villiform projections on the
surface of hairy cells.Elongated villis have a crossing phenomenon.The surface of some hairy cells
appears ruffled projections.
Under transmmisonelectron microscope,there are notonlyvilliformprojections but alsoribosome
layerscomplex(PLC)in the cytoplasm ofhairy cells.

成人T细胞白血病
成人T细胞白血病（AdultTcellleukemia，ATL）是发生在成年人的一种特殊类型的白血病。男性多于
女性。典型病例呈急性或亚急性经过，常有浅表淋巴结肿大，肝脾明显肿大，但无纵隔或胸腺肿瘤。约半数病人
有皮肤改变，呈周身性丘疹或红皮病，皮肤活检可见典型的多形核淋巴细胞（花细胞）浸润。也有以高血钙为首
发表现者、如乏力、嗜睡、恶心、烦渴和多尿等。倘若出现腹水，提示预后恶劣。可有溶骨性损害。
血象贫血相对较轻。白细胞大多增高，常超过10×10/L，可高达200×10/L。白血病性淋巴细胞即多
形核淋巴细胞占10%以上，可高达91%。其形态特征是，胞体大小不等，核呈多形性，扭曲、畸形或分叶状，核
凹陷很深呈两叶、多叶，或呈棒球手套状，或折叠呈花瓣状等复杂形态，故又称“花细胞”（Flowercell）。极
少数者隐约可见1~2个核仁。
骨髓象骨髓受累程度较外周血轻，花细胞浸润不及外周血明显。这一点常有别于一般白血病。
花细胞属T细胞型，有成熟T细胞表面标志。
88
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOG
Adult T cell leukemia
AdultTcell leukemia（ATL)isa special type of leukemias occuringinadults.It ismore common in
male and has an acute or subacute onset.The patients may often present with superficial lymphadenopa-
thy or obvioushepatosplenomegaly but without tumorsof mediastinum andthymus.About half of
patients have skin invo lement,such as systemic papulosis or erythroderma.Skin biopsy reveals the
infiltration ofpolymorphous nuclear lymphocytes(flower cells).Some patients firstly complaint the
symptoms of hypercalcemia such as fatigue,drowsiness,nausea,dipsesis and polyuria.The presence of
ascite indicates poor prognosis.Lytic bone lesions also have been described.
HemogramAnemia is relatively slight.Most patients haveleukocytosiswith a WBCcount higher
than 10×10°/L even up to 200×10°/L.Leukemic lymphocytes (ie,polymorphousnuclear lymphocytes)
have a propotion over 10%,even up to91%.The cells are varying in size.The nuclei are polymorphous,
twisted,malformedor segmentedwith deep introcessions showingtwoor multipleleaves,and may have
ashapeofbaseball gloves or folding corollaceous complex,so that thecells are alsonamed flower cells.
One nucleolus or twonucleoli can be seen in fewcases.
MyelogramTheinvolvementofbonemarrow byflowercellsisnotasobviousasof theperipheral
blood,which is different from other types of leukemias.
Flower cells belong toT lymphocytes,expressingmature T-cell markers.

幼淋巴细胞白血病
幼淋巴细胞白血病（Prolymphocyticleukemia，PLL）是一种罕见的淋巴细胞增殖性疾病。发病年龄多在
50岁以上，中位数为62岁。起病缓慢，以贫血为主要症状，脾脏中、重度肿大，可有肝大。局部淋巴结肿大不
明显或不肿大。分为B细胞幼淋巴细胞和T细胞幼淋巴细胞白血病。
血象轻中度贫血。白细胞总数常增高，偶可高达265×10/L，中位数为84.5×10/L，但也可正常。分
类时幼淋巴细胞增多，占25%~65%。血小板多降低。
骨髓象增生明显活跃，以淋巴细胞为主，主要是幼淋巴细胞。其胞体比小淋巴细胞略大，呈圆形。胞浆较
丰富，嗜碱性，偶含嗜苯胺蓝颗粒。核圆形，染色质浓聚成块或粗细不等，排列不均。常有大而明显的核仁1~
2个。幼淋巴细胞是诊断本病的重要依据。
细胞化学染色POX与NAE均为阴性，PAS染色80%为阳性，ACP阳性但可被酒石酸所抑制，α-萘酚
醋酸酯酶染色（ANAE）阳性。
Prolymphocyticleukemia
Prolymphocytic leukemia (PLL)is a rare type of lymphoproliferative disorders.Most patients are
older than50years old.Themedianage is 62years.Ithasa chroniconset.Mainmanifestation is anemia
withmoderate or severe splenomegaly,sometimeswith hepatomegaly.Lymphadenopathy doesnotexist
or isnotremarkable.It is divided intoB-cell and T-cell PLL
HemogramAnemiaismildormoderate.WBCcountusuallyincreaseswith themedianof84.5x
10°/L, occasionally reaching 265×10°/L. WBC count can be also normal in some patients. The propor-
tion of prolymphocytes increases to 25%~65%.PLT count is oftenreduced.
MyelogramThepatientshaveahypercellularbonemarrowwiththepredominanceoflymphocytes.
Themajorityoflymphocyticcellsareprolymphocyteswhicharelarger thansmalllymphocytes.These
roundprolymphocyteshaveabundantbasophiliccytoplasm with azurophilicgranulessometimes.The
nuclei are round with clumpy chromatin.Coarse or fine chromatin isunsymmetrically arranged.
Prolymphocytesmayhave 1~2largeandobviousnuclei.Thepresence ofprolymphocytesisanimportant
evidence to the diagnosis.
Cytochemistry stainingIt shows thatprolymphocytes arePOX and NAEnegative,PASpositive in
80%ofpatients,ACPpositive whichcan beinhibited by tartaricacidand ANAE positive.

浆细胞白血病
浆细胞白血病（Plasmacellleukemia，PCL）是一种少见类型的白血病。起病较急，呈现白血病的临床表
现或与多发性骨髓瘤临床经过相似，但外周血中浆细胞数大于20%或其绝对值大于2.0×10/L。根据有无多发
性骨髓瘤病史分为继发性和原发性两大类。
血象有不同程度的贫血和血小板减少。白细胞数大于10×10/L，异常的浆细胞常大于20%或其绝对值
大于2.0×10/L。胞体呈圆形或椭圆形，体积较小且大小一致。浆呈灰蓝色，有时边缘着色深，可有细小紫红
色颗粒，偶呈粉红色团块。核圆，偏在，染色质呈细网状。核仁可有可无。继发于多发性骨髓瘤时，幼浆细胞大
小不等，与原发性者截然不同。
骨髓象有核细胞增生明显活跃，以胞体大小相同的较小的幼浆细胞为主，其形态同血象描述。
Plasma Cell Leukemia
Plasma cell leukemia (PCL)is a rare type of leukemias.The disease has an acute onset,presenting
91
图谱
with the clinical manifestations of leukemia or multiple myeloma(MM).However,there are more than
20%of plasma cells in the peripheral blood or an absolute plasma cell count over 2.0x 10/L.PCL is
divided into primary and secondary types according to the absence or presence ofMMhistory.
HemogramAnemia and thrombocytopenia are common in different degrees.WBC count is over 10x
10/L.Abnormal plasma cells are more than 20%or have an absolute count over 2.0x10°/L. The cells
are round or oval in shape,small and homogeneous in size. The cytoplasm is gray-blue and deeply
stained in the margin with some fine purplish-red granules or pink masses. The round and eccentric
nuclei contain fine-reticular chromatin with the presence or absence ofnucleoli.Proplasmacytes are
obviously heterogeneousin size when it is secondary to multiple myeloma,which is completely different
from primary PCL.
MyelogramThe patients have a hypercellular bone marrow.Proplasmacytes predominate and are
small and homogeneous in size just as described above.

慢性粒细胞白血病
慢性粒细胞白血病（Chronicmyelocyticleukemia，CML）多发于青壮年。起病缓慢，症状轻微，常因其
他疾病就诊时发现脾大或白细胞总数明显升高被诊断。早期症状往往是乏力、低热、多汗、体重减轻等代谢亢进
表现或者左上腹不适、食后胀满感。巨脾是最突出的体征，但也有脾不大者。肝脏常轻度肿大，淋巴结肿大较为
少见。胸骨可有压痛。90%以上患者骨髓细胞中存在pH染色体和/或BCR/ABL融合基因。
血象发病早期红细胞和血红蛋白正常，随着病情进展逐渐减低，并可有少数幼红细胞。血小板计数早期大
多正常或增高，晚期则减少。白细胞总数大多明显升高，初诊时常为50.00×10/L，可高达1000.00×10/L，
并可见到各阶段的粒细胞，以中性中幼粒细胞以下各阶段的粒细胞为主，早幼粒与原始粒细胞之和小于10%。加
速期原始粒细胞（I型+Ⅱ型）>10%；急变期原粒+早幼粒≥30%或原始粒细胞（1型+Ⅱ型）或原淋+幼
淋或原单+幼单》20%。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分降低。嗜酸和嗜碱性粒细胞增高，淋巴细胞和单核细胞百分
数减低。
骨髓象
有核细胞增生明显活跃或极度活跃，以粒系增生为主，粒红比值明显升高。中性中幼粒以下各阶段
细胞明显增多，主要是晚幼及中幼粒细胞增多，其次是早幼粒、杆状核和分叶核粒细胞。慢性期原始粒细胞（1
93
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
型+Ⅱ型）<10%；加速期>10%；急变期原始粒细胞（I型+Ⅱ型）或原淋+幼淋或原单+幼单>20%，或原
始粒细胞+早幼粒细胞≥50%。嗜酸和嗜碱性粒细胞增多，幼红细胞减少。巨核细胞早期增多，晚期减少。
Chronic myelocytic leukemia
Chronic myelocytic leukemia(CML) most commonly occurs in young and middle-aged adults with
and leukocytosis because ofmedical evaluation for other diseases.Early symptoms includevigorous
metabolism presentations(fatigue,low fever, sweats and weight loss)or discomfort and fullness feeling
after eating in the left upper quadrant of the body.Massive splenomegaly is the most outstanding sign
though a few patients have been diagnosed without it. Slight hepatomegaly is common.The enlargement
have the Philadelphia chromosome (pH) and/or the BCR/ABL infusion genes.
Hemogram In the early stage of the disease,RBC and HGB are normal.Anemia occurs with the
progression of disease.Nucleated red blood cells can be seen in some cases.Platelet count is normal or
elevated initially,and then decrease in the late stage of CML.Leukocytosis is common at the time of
diagnosis.Leukocyte count ranges from50.0×10/L to1000x10°/L.Granulocytes in all differential
stages arepresent.Myelocytes,metamyelocytes,stab and segmentedneutrophils usually predominate.
Myeloblasts and promyelocytes have a proportion less than 10%.In accelerated phase,blasts (type I +
type I)are over 10%.In blast crisis phase blasts and promyelocytes are>30%,or blasts>20%,or
lymphoblasts and prolymphocytes>20%,or monoblasts and promonocytes>20%.NAP activity is low or
absent.Basophilia,eosinophilia,relatively decreasedpercents ofmonocytes and lymphocytes can be seen.
increasedgranulocytic/erythroidratio.Most granulocytes areneutrophiliccells which arematurer than
promyelocytes,especiallyneutrophilicmetamyelocytes andmyelocytes,and then promyelocytes,stab and
segmented cells.Blasts (type I + type II) have a proportion less than 10% in chronic phase.In accelerated
phase,blasts have a proportion over 10%.Inblast crisis phase blasts are >20%,or lymphoblasts and
prolymphocytes>20%,orblastsand promyelocytes>50%.Basophilia and eosinophilia arepresent.
Normoblasts decreases.The count ofmegakaryocytes is elevated in the early stage and decreased in the
late stage.

慢性粒细胞白血病急性变
慢性粒细胞白血病自诊断后1～4年，约70%病人发生疾病变异，出现急性白血病的血象、骨髓象和临床表
现，称为急变期，简称慢粒急变。临床表现有原因不明的发热，用抗生素治疗无效，体重减轻，骨骼疼痛，贫血
加重，脾脏进行性肿大，用原来治疗慢粒药物无效。血象中嗜碱性粒细胞明显增多，血小板减少。经骨髓穿刺可
以证实急变。临床上最常见的急变类型是急性粒细胞白血病变，其次为急性淋巴细胞白血病变。
慢粒急变的诊断标准：①原始粒细胞（1型+Ⅱ型）或原淋+幼淋、或原单+幼单在外周血或骨髓中≥20%；
②外周血内原始粒细胞+早幼粒细胞≥30%；③骨髓内原始粒细胞+早幼粒细胞≥50%；④伴髓外原始细胞浸润。
Blastcrisis of CML
About 70%of the patientswith CMLwill have a progress in the disease after 1~4years of the
diagnosis,presenting blood and bone marrowfindings and clinical manifestations which are corresponding
to acute leukemias.It is called blastic crisis of CML with the abbreviation CML-BC.The patients have
progressive anemia and splenomegaly.Traditional anti-CML drugs have no more effects. Basophil count
is significantly elevated andPLT count is decreased in the peripheral blood.CML-BC can be identified
bybonemarrowaspiration.Themostcommon type of CML-BCis acutemyelocytictransformation,the
secondisacutelymphoblastictransformation.
Diagnostic criteria of CML-BC:
①myeloblasts (typeI+typeI),orlymphoblasts andprolymphocytes,or monoblasts andpromonocytes
are>20%in the peripheralblood or bone marrow;myeloblasts and promyelocytes>30%in the
peripheral blood;③myeloblasts andpromyelocytes>50%in the bone marrow；with extramedullary
infiltration of blasts.

慢性淋巴细胞白血病
慢性淋巴细胞白血病（Chroniclymphocyticleukemia，CLL）是淋巴细胞系中某些免疫功能不全的淋巴
细胞恶性增生性疾病。50岁以上发病，男性多于女性，很多病人血象已经发生明显改变但尚无自觉症状。浅表
淋巴结特别是颈部淋巴结肿大常为首发症状，脾脏轻、中度肿大，晚期则出现贫血等症状。约10%病人出现黄痘
（并发自身免疫性溶血性贫血）。偶见皮肤浸润，如紫红色或棕红色结节，周身皮肤可以发红、增厚。14%病人胸
骨有压痛。本病的大多数为CD5+的B细胞型，少数为T细胞型。
血象白细胞总数升高，波动在（15~50）×10/L之间，“成熟淋巴细胞”>60%，可高达90%以上，其绝
对值>6.0×10°/L。这种白血病性成熟淋巴细胞的形态犹如正常的小淋巴细胞，有时核染色质呈不规则聚集。红
细胞和血红蛋白早期不减低，若并发自身免疫性溶血性贫血时则明显减低，同时网织红细胞升高，可出现幼稚红
细胞。晚期血小板常减少。
很少，一般不超过5%。粒系、红系和巨核系细胞均减少。
细胞化学染色淋巴细胞糖原染色阳性，中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分正常或稍增高。
ChronicLymphocytic Leukemia
Chronic lymphocytic leukemia (CLL)is a malignant lymphoproliferative disorder. CLL cells are
immunoincompetent.Thediseaseoccurschieflyinmenmore than50yearsold.Manypatientshaveonly
changes in the peripheral blood without symptoms.The enlargement of superficial lymph nodes,espe-
cially cervical lymphnodes,is commonlythe earliest symptom.Mild or moderate splenomegaly can exist.
Anemia appears in the late stage of the disease.10%of the patients present with jaundice (complicated
with AIHA). Skin infiltration occurs in rare cases,which shows purplish-red or brownish-red nodes
with skin erythema and thickening.14%of thepatientshave sternal tenderness.Most CLLcells are CD5+
Blymphocytes,and others are T lymphocytes.
HemogramThe total number of wBCincreases and ranges from 15x10/L to 50x10/L.
"Mature lymphocyte”count is >60%,even up to 90%or in some cases with an absolute number over
6.0x10/L.The leukemicmature lymphocytes look like normal small lymphocytes.The chromatin
aggregates irregularly sometimes.In the early stage of the disease,RBC and HGB are normal. Anemia
occurs when CLL is complicated by AIHA,presenting increasing reticulocytes and immature RBC.
Thrombocytopeniaoccursin thelatestageofthedisease
MyelogramThepatients havea hypercellular or very hypercellular bonemarrowwith the
predominance of lymphocytes which are often >40%,even up to 90%~100% in some cases.Lymphoblasts
and prolymphocytes are few,usually not over 5%.Granulocytic,erythroid and megakaryocytic cells are
alldecreased.
alittle increased.

慢性中性粒细胞白血病
慢性中性粒细胞白血病（Chronicneutrophilicleukemia，CNL）属骨髓增殖性疾病。成人发病，中位数
年龄为48岁。主要临床表现为乏力，轻度贫血，少数可有出血倾向。脾脏明显肿大，常有肝大，浅表淋巴结均
无明显肿大。可有胸骨压痛。
血象白细胞总数持续升高，常>30×10/L，可高达70×10/L，中性粒细胞占87%以上，绝对值>14×
10/L。成熟的中性粒细胞胞浆中有粗大的毒性样颗粒，部分有空泡，偶见分叶过多现象。极少出现中性中、晚
幼粒细胞。嗜酸及嗜碱性粒细胞不增多。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分明显升高，常>300分。无pH染色体。美
蓝染色时，部分中性粒细胞内可见到Dohl小体。血红蛋白轻度或重度降低。血小板大多正常，少数可增高，偶
可减少。
骨髓象有核细胞增生明显或极度活跃，粒系明显增多，以成熟中性粒细胞为主，中性杆状核与分叶核粒
细胞常>50%；中性中、晚幼粒细胞为20%左右。原始或早幼粒细胞比例不高，嗜酸和嗜碱性粒细胞不增多。
红系常明显受抑。巨核细胞大多正常，少数比例增多，也可减少，偶见小巨核细胞，血小板正常或轻度增多，
少数可明显增多。
与慢性粒细胞白血病区别，CNL时：①白血病细胞仅局限于成熟的中性粒细胞；②胞浆中粗大的毒性样颗
粒增多；③嗜酸和嗜碱性粒细胞减少或阙如；④中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分明显升高；③pH染色体阴性。
Chronic Neutrophilic Leukemia
Chronic neutrophilicleukemia(CNL）is a chronic myeloproliferative disorder.It occurs in adults.
Median age at diagnosis is 48years.Themostcommon clinical manifestationsinclude fatigability and
mild anemia.Hemorrhagic tendency is present ina fewpatients.Splenomegaly is obvious with hepatomegaly
frequently.Superficial lymphadenopathy occursrarely and sternal tenderness is common.
HemogramThe total leukocyte count is always elevated,often exceeding 30x10°/L,even as high
as70×10°/L.Neutrophils are over 87percentof thewhite cellswith anabsolute count exceeding14x
10°/L.Mature granulocytes contain coarse toxic particles in the cytoplasm with vacuoles partly,and
present hypersegmented occasionally.Myelocytesandmetamyelocytes arerarelypresent.Basophils and
eosinophils are usually not increased.Neutrophil alkaline phosphase(NAP)activityisvirtually increased,
often exceeds 300 scores.ThepH chromsome is absent.A part ofneutrophils show Dohle bodies when
stained with methylene blue.Hemoglobin is slightly or severely decreased.Platelet count usually is
102
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOG
normal or slightlyincreased,and occasionally decreased.
granulopoiesis,most ofwhich arematureneutrophils.Stab and segmentedneutrophils are over 50%
neutrophilicmyelocytes andmetamyelocytes areabout 20%.Theproportionofmyeloblastsandpromyelocytes
is not high,and eosinophils and basophils are not increased.Erythropoiesis is markedly inhibited.
Whereas,megakaryocytes arenormal in most patients,increased or decreased in a few patients.Occasion
ally small megakaryocytes can be sen.Platelet count may be normal or slightly elevated,and even
significantly increased in a few cases.
Differingfrom chronicmyelocytic leukemia,CNLis characterized by ①leukemiccells are limitedin
matureneutrophils;coarse toxicparticlesinthecytoplasm areincreased;③eosinophils andbasophils
are reduced or absent; the score of NAP activity is significantly high;pH chromsome is negative.

原发性血小板增多症
原发性血小板增多症（Essentialthrombocythemia，ET）又称为出血性血小板增多症，属于骨髓增殖
性疾病。40岁以上多发，男性多于女性。主要表现为血小板的持续增多，伴有其他造血系统轻度增生。有程
度不等的出血和/或血栓形成症状。出血较常见于皮肤黏膜和胃肠道。血栓形成多见于肢体血管，表现为手
足麻木、发细、肿胀甚或坏疽。脑血管受累时则有相应改变。脾和肝脏常轻度肿大，部分病人的脾脏可因反
复梗死而缩小。
血象血小板计数大于1000×10/L，常在（1000~3000）×10/L之间，最高可达（10000~15000）×10/
L。涂片两端血小板常聚集成片，大小不一，并可出现巨形血小板，偶见巨核细胞或其碎片。白细胞总数常升高，
分类基本正常或中性粒细胞增高，可见各阶段的幼粒细胞。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶活性升高。约1/3病人红细胞
可略增高。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃或明显活跃。巨核细胞明显增生，大多为成熟型巨核细胞，原、幼巨核细胞均
可增多，胞体大，胞浆丰富。血小板显著增多且聚集成片、成堆。
Essential thrombocythemia
Essential thrombocythemia（ET)isalsonamedhemorrhagic thrombocythemia,belongingtomyelo-
proliferative disorders.The disease commonly occurs in persons older than 40 years,and has a male
predominance.Mainmanifestationisthepersistentincreaseofplateletswithmildhyperplasiaoferyth
ropoiesis andmyelopoiesis.The patients have symptoms of bleeding and(or) thrombosisin different
extents.Bleeding commonlyhappensin skin,mucosa and gastrointestinal tract.Thrombosis often occurs
in the vessels of extremities,which is characterized bynumbness,swelling and cyanosis,even gangrene
of hands and feet.When cerebral vessels are involved,concordant symptoms appear.The patients often
havemild enlargementofspleenandliver.Becauseofrepeated embolism,somepatientspresentwitha
diminished spleen.
HemogramThe count ofplateletsusually is over 1000x10/L,mostly between1000×10/L and
3000x10°/L, sometimes even up to (10000~15000)x10/L.Platelets usually vary in size and congregate
appear in rare cases.The total number of WBC increases with normal differential count or increased
neutrophils.Immature granulocytes in every stage can be seen.NAP activity of granulocytes is high and
one in third of the patients have an slightly increased RBC.
MyelogramThe patients havea hypercellularbonemarrowwithmarked hyperplasia of megakaryocytes.
The majority of them are mature megakaryocytes. Megakaryoblasts and promegakaryocytes also increase.
They are large and have abundant cytoplasm.Platelets are increasing and aggregate into clumps.

真性红细胞增多症
真性红细胞增多症（Polycythemiavera，PV）是一种原因不明的红细胞系统异常增生为主的慢性骨髓增
殖性疾病。常伴造血细胞一系以上的异常。其临床特点是发病缓慢，病程较长，红细胞明显增多，血容量绝对增
加，红细胞压积增高，常伴有白细胞和血小板增多。皮肤及黏膜红紫色，脾肿大。
血象红细胞大多数（7~10）×10/L，血红蛋白（180~240）g/L，白细胞大多数高于正常，约半数为（10~
31）×10°/L，极少数大于50×10/L，血小板计数增多，在（300~1000）×10/L之间。
骨髓象有核细胞增生活跃或明显活跃，粒、红及巨核细胞三系增生，尤以红系及巨核细胞系增生为显著。
Polycythemia Vera
Polycythemiavera(PV)is anacquiredmyeloproliferativedisorder resultingfromclonalmultipoten-
tialhemopoieticstemcells.Itisoftencomplicatedwithabnormalitiesofseveralseriesofhemopoieticcells.
The clinical features present with a chronic onset,long course of the disease,markedlyincreased
105
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
erythrocytesand hematocrit.Itisfrequentlycomplicatedwith the increasementofWBCandPLT.Skin
andmucosa is amaranthine and thespleen is enlarged.
Hemogram Erythrocytes ofmost patients vary from 7x102/L to 10x1012/L.Hemoglobin is
（180~240)g/L.WBCcountismostly increasedwith（10~31)×10°/Linhalfpatients andmore than50x
10°/L in a few patients.Platelet count is increased,ranging from 300x 10/L to 1000 x10/L.
MyelogramBonemarrow ishypercellular or markedlyhypercellular.Granulocytic,erythrocytic
andmegakaryocytic series are allhyperplastic,especially thefirst twolineages.

原发性骨髓纤维化
原发性骨髓纤维化（Primarymyelofibrosis，PMF）是原因不明的骨髓弥漫性、非均匀一致的纤维组织增
生以及主要在脾脏、其次在肝脏髓外造血（或称髓外化生）的一种骨髓增殖性疾病。典型临床表现是，中老年发
病，幼粒、幼红细胞性贫血，脾脏常显著肿大以及不同程度的骨质硬化。
血象大多数病人均有贫血，属正细胞正色素型贫血。成熟红细胞大小不一，常可见到泪滴状红细胞，具有
辅助诊断价值。可见不同阶段的幼红细胞。网织红细胞常偏高，在2%～5%之间。白细胞总数一般在（10～20）×
10°/L之间，>50×10/L也不少见。以成熟粒细胞为主，可见10%~20%的幼稚粒细胞，主要是中、晚幼粒细
胞，也可见到早幼粒和原始粒细胞。晚期白细胞数可减少。血小板在疾病早期增多，随病情进展逐渐减少，可见
巨型血小板和巨核细胞或其碎片。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分大多增高。
骨髓象多部位骨髓穿刺常不易抽出髓液，俗称“干抽”，亦是本病特征之一。疾病早期，骨髓造血细胞仍
可增生，尤其是粒系与巨核系增生，但晚期时有核细胞增生低下。
骨髓活检骨髓活体病理切片检查是确诊本病的必要条件，显示网状纤维和/或胶原纤维增生。
Primary Myelofibrosis
Primary myelofibrosis（PMF）is a myeloproliferative disorderwithout definite causes,characterized
by unevenly diffusehyperplasiaof fibroustissueinbonemarrow,and extramedullaryhemapoiesismainly
occuring in the spleen,then the liver.It is a disorder of old patients,presenting with myelocyte-
normoblast anemia,marked splenomegaly and osteosclerosisin differentextents.
HemogramMostpatientspresentwithanormocytic-normochromicanemiaandprominentanisocytosis.
Teardrop-shaped red blood cells are present and have an assisted value in the diagnosis.Immature
erythrocytes in all different stages appear in the blood film.Reticulocyte count is elevated with a range
of2%to5%.TotalWBCcount usuallyis10×10/L to20x10/L.Thecasesexceeding50×10°/Lare
not rare.Most cells are mature granulocytes,but 10% to 20%of immature granulocytes can be detected
with themajorityofmyelocytesandmetamyelocytes.Promyelocytesandmyeloblastscanalsobeseen.
WBC count may be decreased in the late stage.Platelet count appears tobe high in the early stage,but
as the diseaseprogresses it can fall to very low level.Giant platelets,giantmegakaryocytes and their
fragmentscan be found.NAPactivityis elevated inmost patients.
Myelogram The marrow is often difficult or impossible to asprite,it is called “dry tap”,which is
oneof the characteristics of the disease.Thepatientsin the early stage show a hyperplastichemapoiesis of
bone marrow,especially granulocytic and megakaryocytic series,whereas hypoplastic in the late stage.
displays anincrease of reticular and(or)collagen fibers.

骨髓增生异常综合征
骨髓增生异常综合征（myelodysplasticsyndrome，MDS）是造血干细胞的克隆性疾病。临床表现以难于
纠正的贫血为主，可伴有白细胞和/或血小板减少，同时伴有病态造血为特点的一组血液病综合征。
一、MDS分型
1982年FAB协作组将MDS分为五型。
1.难治性贫血（refractoryanemia，RA）
2.环状铁粒幼细胞性难治性贫血（RAwithringsideroblasts，RAS）
3.原始粒细胞过多性难治性贫血（RAwithexcessofblasts,RAEB）
4.转化中原始粒细胞过多性难治性贫血（RAEBintransformation，RAEB-T）
5.慢性粒-单核细胞白血病（chronicmyelomonocyticleukemia，CMML）
多（占20%~40%，绝对值>1.0×10/L）。近来FAB协作组已将CMML划为慢性髓系白血病的一个亚型。

三.MDS诊断
外周血一系、二系或三系血细胞减少，偶有白细胞增多。骨髓中至少有二系病态造血，则可诊断MDS。但

7/7q-，9q-及20q-。

MyelodysplasticSyndrome
Myelodysplastic syndrome (MDs）isa clonal stem cell disorder.It is a group of the clinical syndrome
presentingwith the combination of anemia difficult to correct,leukopenia and/or thrombocytopenia
with dysplastic hemopoiesis.
1.Classification of MDS
FAB Cooperative Group propose MDS as five subtypes in 1982.
①Refractory anemia,RA
②RA with ring sideroblasts,RAS
③RA withexcessofblasts,RAEB
RAEBin transformation,RAEB-T
Chronicmyelomonocyticleukemia,CMML
The domestic classification is proposed to be four subtypes,namely RA,RAS,RAEB,and RAEB-
109
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
T.CMML is assigned to each of 1~4 subtypes,which is complicated with increased monocyte count in
the peripheral blood (20%~40%,absolute count>1.0x10/L).The FAB Cooperative Group recently
reclassifies CMML as a subtype of CML(chronic myelocytic leukemia).

3.Diagnosis of MDS
The diagnosis should be considered in the patients with cytopenia of one,two orall three cell
lineages in theperipheral blood and dysplastichemopoiesisof atleast two cell lineagesin thebone
marrow.However,erythroleukemic leukemia,atypicalaplastic anemia and secondary MDS should be
distinguished.The most common chromosomal changes in MDS are -5/5q-,+8,-7/7q-,9q-and 20q-.

恶性组织细胞病
恶性组织细胞病（Malignanthistiocytosis，MH），简称恶组，是组织细胞异常增生的恶性疾病。其病理特
点是在肝脾、骨髓、淋巴结等器官和组织中出现异常组织细胞灶性增生，偶可单独累及淋巴结。常伴有明显的血
细胞被吞噬现象。恶组细胞多数是T淋巴细胞系，其次是B淋巴细胞系的大淋巴细胞瘤，少数是来源于单核-巨
噬细胞系统的真性恶性组织细胞病。多发于青壮年，长期发热，以高热为主，进行性衰竭、出血和黄疽。肝脾和
淋巴结肿大，全血细胞减少（偶见白细胞增多）。少数病例有浆膜腔积液等。
血象不同程度的贫血且进行性加重，初诊时血红蛋白降低可能不甚明显，但晚期时常低至（50～60）
g/L以下。白细胞计数在初诊时虽有增高或正常，但晚期时几乎均减少，尤其是中性粒细胞进行性减少。部分病
例可有少量幼粒和幼红细胞。血小板大多减少。网织红细胞计数正常或略高。在血片边缘及尾部可有少量组织细
胞。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分减低。
骨髓象找到异常组织细胞和/或多核组织细胞是诊断本病的主要依据，特别是对多核巨组织细胞有诊断意
义。
Malignant Histiocytosis
Malignant histiocytosis (MH) is a malignant disease of abnormally proliferative histiocytes.Patho-
logicalexamination revealsfocal proliferation of abnomal histiocytes in the liver,spleen,bonemarrow
and lymph nodes,occasionally only involving lymph nodes. The disease is ususally accompaniedby the
phenomenon that abnormal histiocytesmarkedlyphagocytose blood cells.Mostmalignant histiocytes are
of T-lymphocyte origin,then large lymphoma cells of B-lymphocyte.In fact,malignant histiocytes
coming from mononuclear-phagocytic system is onlyin theminority.The disease occurs more oftenin
failure,hemorrhage,jaundice,hepatosplenomegly,lymphadenopathy andpancytopenia(occasionalleukocytosis）.
Afew cases can presentwith serosal effusion.
Hemogram Progressive anemia in varying degrees can be found.Although hemoglobin is not
obviously decreased at the time of diagnosis,it is often declined under (50~60)g/L in thelate stage.
Similarly,WBC count may be increased or normal at the time of diagnosis,but almost all cases have
leukopenia in the late stagewith a progressiveneutropenia.Apartof cases mayhavea few immature
granulocytes and erythroblasts.Plateles are decreased in most patients.Reticulocyte count isnormal or
activity is low.
MyelogramThe diagnosis of the disease depends on the detection of abnormal histiocytes and/or
giantpolynucleated histiocytes.Especially,finding the latter havea diagnostic significance.

反应性组织细胞增多症
伤寒、栗粒型结核、败血症和其他感染性疾病及某些结缔组织病时，骨髓中有时也可见到较多的组织
细胞，称反应性组织细胞增多症（Reactivehistiocytosis）。本病与恶性组织细胞病不同点是：①有原发病
可寻，且原发病被控制后组织细胞减少或消失；②有原发病的血清学和细菌学检查的各自特点；③中性粒
细胞碱性磷酸酶积分大多增高；④骨髓中组织细胞虽然增多，但胞体大小、形态比较一致，偶见异常组织
细胞，无多核巨型组织细胞。
Reactive Histiocytosis
Reactivehistiocytosisrefers to theincreased histiocytesinbonemarrow of thepatientswho
suffer from typhoid fever,miliary tuberculosis,septicemia,some infectious and connective tissue
diseases.The characteristics ofthedisease distinguishedfrommalignanthistiocytosisareas fellowings:
①It is associated with a primary disease.The histiocytes decrease or disappear as the primary

diseaseiscontrolled.Italsopossessesserologicalandbacteriologicalfeaturesoftheprimarydisease
respectively.③NAPactivityisincreased in most cases.Increasedhistiocytes in the bone marrow
arerelatively identical in size and shape.Abnormalhistiocytes can be occasionally found but nogiant
polynucleated histiocytes.

噬血细胞综合征
噬血细胞综合征（Hemophagocytic syndrome，HPS）是单核-巨噬细胞系统的疾病之一。可分为以下儿
种：①爆发性噬血细胞综合征，酷似恶组，病情区险，多短期内死亡。②感染相关性噬血细胞综合征（Infection-
relatedhemophagocyticsyndrome，IHPS），多见于儿童，常由各种病毒、细菌和霉菌感染所引起。③家族性
噬血细胞综合征，为常染色体隐性遗传性疾病。
血象血红蛋白、白细胞和血小板均可有不同程度的减低。白细胞分类中淋巴细胞相对增高。易见异型淋巴
细胞。
骨髓象增生正常或减低。易见巨噬细胞，胞体大，吞噬各种血细胞。
Hemophagocytic syndrome
Hemophagocytic syndrome (HPs) is a disease of mononuclear-phagocytic system.It can be
divided into three types: ①fulminant HPS,which is as severe as malignant histocytosis,and has a
122
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
poor prognosis and the patients will die in the short term.infection-related HPS,which mostly
Occurs in children,and is often causedby varying viral,bacterial or fungi infections. family HPS,
which is an autosomal recessive disease.
HemogramHGB,WBCand PLT decrease in different degrees.The proportion of lymphocytes
in the differential count of total WBC increases.Atypical lymphocytes are easy to find.
MyelogramThe patients have a normally proliferative or hypocellular bone marrow. Some
macrophagocytes can be seen easily.They are large and phagocytize various blood cells.

多发性骨髓瘤
多发性骨髓瘤（Multiplemyeloma，MM）是浆细胞异常增生的恶性肿瘤。发病年龄以50~70岁居多，男
性多于女性。临床表现有骨痛，尤其腰骶部疼痛是本病的主要症状之一；进行性贫血；病理性骨折，如可有肋骨
多发性骨折及椎体压缩性骨折；骨骼局部肿块，质坚硬，大小不等，多见于颅骨、锁骨、肋骨和胸骨等处；血清
中出现M蛋白，球蛋白增高和白/球蛋白比值倒置；尿本-周蛋白可阳性，蛋白尿及管型尿；区线的典型病变
为圆形、边界清楚的如穿凿样溶骨性损害或广泛性骨质疏松。
血象轻中度贫血，属正细胞正色素性贫血，红细胞常排列成串，形如钱。白细胞和血小板计数正常，但
晚期呈全血细胞减少。外周血有时可见到少数幼粒细胞和幼红细胞，偶可见到少量骨髓瘤细胞。当外周血骨髓瘤
细胞>20%或绝对值>2.0×10/L时，称浆细胞白血病。
骨髓象粒系、红系和巨核系细胞大致正常，主要是骨髓瘤细胞增多，至少占有核细胞10%～30%，最多可
达95%。胞体直径为9-58um，圆形、椭圆形或不规则形。核呈圆形或椭圆形，偏在，偶见核分叶，有时可见
2-5个核，染色质较疏松，也可凝集成块，但不呈辐射状排列。有1~2个核仁。胞浆灰蓝至深蓝色，也可呈紫
红色，可有少数嗜苯胺蓝颗粒。偶见胞浆内含有火红色的嗜酸球状包涵体，即Russell小体，称Mot细胞。这种
Russell小体染色时被溶解形成空泡。当胞浆中有红色片状和滴状物时称“火焰细胞”。有时胞浆内可见红色的棒
状小体，称晶状体。
根据骨髓瘤细胞分化程度及其形态特点，可将骨髓瘤大致分为：①浆细胞型。细胞分化成熟，大小如正常浆
细胞。染色质致密但不呈车辐状凝集，核偏在。胞浆丰富呈蓝色；②幼浆细胞型。以幼浆细胞和原浆细胞为主，
瘤细胞畸形显著。易见多核。胞浆内偶见粉红色Russell小体；③网状细胞样骨髓瘤细胞型。胞体较大，胞浆呈
灰紫色，可有嗜苯胺蓝颗粒。核圆形或椭圆形，染色质不均呈网状。可见核仁。
有的瘤细胞颇似幼红细胞，故又有幼红细胞型骨髓瘤之称。
Multiple Myeloma
Multiple myeloma (MM） is a malignancy of neoplastic plasma cells.The average ages of most
patients are from 50 to 70years.The disease occursmoreofteninmen than in women.Clinical
manifestations include bone pain (lumbosacral pain is one of themost common symptoms);progressive
tumor mass of bone,being hard and varying in size and involving skull,clavicles,ribs and sternum
frequently:presentation of M-component in serum,increasingglobulin and inverted albumin/globulin
ratio;positiveurinaryBence-Jonesprotein,proteinuria and cylinderuria;typically punched-outlytic
bonelesionswhich areroundwith clearboundaries,and widely osteoporosis on roentgenogram.
HemogramMild to moderate anemia is present with erythrocytes arranged in a“stack of coins"
Sometimes afewimmaturegranulocytes and erythroblastsmaybepresentin theperipheralblood
occasionallywithafewmyelomacells.Oncemyelomacellsexceed20%intheperipheralbloodortheir
absolute countismore than 2.0×10/L,the disease is defined as plasma cell leukemia.
MyelogramGranulocytic,erythrocyticand megakaryocyticseriesarenearlynormal,except that
increasingmyelomacellsarepresentwhichaccountatleast10%~20%ofthenucleatedcells,oreven as
highas95%.Thecellsare9μm~58μmindiameterandround,ellipticorirregularinshape.Thenuclei
areroundorellipticandplacedeccentrically withnuclear segmentationsoccasionally,2~5nucleicanbe
formation.1~2nucleoli are visible.Thecytoplasm isgray-blue to darkblue,orpurplish-redwith a few
azurophilic granules.The cell containing scarleteosinophilicglobular inclusion named Russell bodyis
called Mott cell. The Russellbody is easy to be dissolved intovacuoles by staining.The cell with red
lamellar and guttate substancein the cytoplasmisnamedflammingcell.Redrod-likebodiespresentin
124
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
the cytoplasm are called lens.
According to the differential degrees andmorphologiccharacteristicsofmyeloma cells,myeloma can
be classified into:1.Plasmacyte type: The myeloma cells have high differentiation and are normal in size.
The chromatin is dense but not arranged in radiating formation.The nuclei are eccentially placed.The
cytoplasm is abundant and stained blue.2.Proplasmacyte type:Proplasmacytes and plasmablasts are in
themajority withmarkedmalformation.Themyeloma cells frequentlyhavemultiplenucleiandocca-
sionally contain pink Russell bodies in the cytoplasm.3.Reticulocytoid myeloma cell type:The myeloma
cells are big in size.The gray-purple cytoplasm contains azurophilic granules.The nuclei are round or
ellipticwithunevenlyreticular chromatin andvisiblenucleoli.
Some myeloma cells are resemblewith erythroblasts.Therefore,the disease also is called erythro-
blast-typemyeloma.
