原发性巨球蛋白血症
原发性巨球蛋白血症（Waldenstrommacroglobulinemia）是恶性浆细胞病中较少见的一种类型，由来自B
淋巴细胞的具有合成和分泌IgM能力的浆细胞发生恶变所致。本病发生于老年，以60～70岁多见。贫血是最常
见的症状，随病情进展可出现肝脾和淋巴结肿大、轻度出血倾向。血液黏滞性增高，常有眼底出血和静脉曲张。
血清中单克隆IgM>10g/L及骨髓中淋巴样浆细胞浸润是诊断本病的必要依据。
血象贫血为正细胞正色素性，红细胞呈婚钱状排列。白细胞轻度减少或正常，少数病例可增高，分类时淋
巴细胞和单核细胞增多。少数病人血小板减少。外周血有时可见到少量（<5%）不典型幼浆细胞。
骨髓象淋巴样浆细胞显著增多，其形态似淋巴细胞。胞浆少，嗜碱性，灰蓝色，其中含有糖原染色阳性的颗粒。
核呈椭圆形或不规则形，染色质致密浓集，可见1~2个核仁，此外，可有裸核的小淋巴细胞、网状细胞和浆细胞。
Waldenstrom Macroglobulinemia
Waldenstrom macroglobulinemia isa rare type ofmalignant plasma cell disorders.It isa B-
lymphoplasmacytemalignancyinwhich thereisabnormalproductionandsecretionofamonoclonalIgM
protein by plasma cells.Thediseaseismore common in olderpatients who generallyare in the sixth or
seventhdecadeof theirlife.The most frequent symptom is anemia.Thepatients usuallypresentwith
hepatosplenomegaly,lymphadenopathyandmildbleeding tendancyasthediseasedevelops.Additionally,
the patients have hyperviscosity and often are noted to have retinal hemorrhage andvaricosis.Serum
monoclonalIgMexceeding10g/L and infiltration of lymphoidplasmacytesin themarrow are essential to
the diagnosis.
HemogramAnemia are usually normocytic and normochromatic.Erythrocytes show rouleaux
formation.Leukocyte countis slightlydecreasedornormalwith increased lymphocytesandmonocytes.
afew atypticalproplasmacytes（<5%)appearin theperipheralblood.
MyelogramLymphoid plasmacytespredominantly increase.They are similar to lymphocytes in
shape.The scanty cytoplasm is basophilic and stainedgray-blue with Periodic Acid-Schiffpositive
granules. The nuclei are elliptic or irregular in shape with condensed chromatin and 12nucleoli.In
addition,small nude-nuclear lymphocytes,reticulocytes andplasmacytes can be seen.

骨髓转移瘤
骨髓转移瘤（Metastatictumorsinbonemarrow）的临床特点是：（1）有或没有肿瘤的既往史；（2）周
身或局限性骨骼疼痛（70%），常以腰骶部和下肢为主；（3）几乎均有不同程度的贫血，重则可伴有微血管病性
溶血性贫血；（4）原因不明的发热（36%）；（5）皮肤黏膜出血（24%），甚至发生慢性DIC；（6）进行性消
瘦（34%）；（7）骨骼压痛是重要的体征（24%），以胸骨、肋骨和脊柱为最多；（8）血沉常增快，有时可达110mmH2O；
（9）骨骼×线检查可出现溶骨性改变，但晚于细胞学所见；（10）因本病时常并发继发性骨髓纤维化，采取骨
髓时易出现“干抽”现象。所以临床上疑似本病，而抽取骨髓时又不成功。更应注意检查每张涂片，以免漏诊。
血象90%以上病例血红蛋白呈不同程度的减低，白细胞总数可低至2.8×10/L，也可高达42.0×10/L，
约2/3病例可见幼红和/或幼粒细胞。幼粒细胞以中、晚幼粒为主，早幼粒较少，偶见原始粒细胞。幼红细胞以
中、晚幼红为主，多少不一，计数100个细胞可见幼红1～97个。嗜酸性粒细胞一般不高。网织红细胞正常或增
多。血小板减少者占47.6%，增多者占52.4%。中性粒细胞碱性磷酸酶积分常增高。
骨髓象瘤细胞多聚集成团或片状，少数散在，偶为弥漫性分布。其分布形式似与有核细胞增生程度有关：
增生低下时，瘤细胞多聚集成团且分布在涂片的头、尾及边缘部；增生活跃时少数瘤细胞团或瘤细胞呈条索状排
列，混杂于正常骨髓细胞成分中，易被忽略。粒系统常有中毒颗粒和空泡。巨核细胞可增多且有成熟受阻现象，
亦可明显减低或缺如。可见盔形、三角形等破碎红细胞。
骨髓中常见的瘤细胞有下述三种：
1.鳞状细胞癌，简称鳞癌鳞癌细胞主要源于上皮组织，好发于皮肤、眼、耳、鼻、喉、口腔、宫颈、食
道和阴茎等部位。其特点是，胞体大，直径在15～90μum不等，多散在，成团者较少。细胞呈多形性，可为蝌蚪
形、不规则形、圆形和蛇形等。核大，圆形或椭圆形，常居中，少数偏在。染色质丰富，深染，呈粗颗粒状或固
缩成团块状。核膜增厚，但核仁一般不明显。胞浆丰富，嗜酸，有时可见空泡。
2.腺癌常源于体内各种腺体组织。腺癌细胞的主要形态特点是，常排列成腺腔样或乳头状，细胞分界不
太清楚。胞体较大，直径17～26um，形态、大小较一致，呈圆形或柱状。核大，常偏在，染色质呈颗粒状，易
见核仁。胞浆量少，染蓝色。有时胞浆有明显的黏液空泡，见于印戒样细胞癌。
3.小细胞未分化癌来源于鳞状上皮或柱状上皮的基底层，分化程度低，恶性度高。其主要特点是，常排
列成带状或条索状，癌细胞常聚集成团。胞体较小，常为类圆形或梭形。核较大，核浆比例核占优势，染色质丰
富，深染。一般无核仁。大多数细胞几乎无胞浆。

HemogramMorethan90%ofcasespresentwithhypohemoglobulinindifferentdegrees.Leukocyte
count may decrease as low as 2.8x10°/Lor increase as high as 42x10/L.Erythroblasts and/or

usuallyiselevated.
MyelogramNeoplasticcellsmainlygatherintomassesorpatches.Theyareuncommonlyscattered
or occasionally diffusely distributed.The distribution seems tobe correlatedwith the proliferative degrees
of nucleated cells.When marrow is hypoplastic,theneoplastic cells are frequently aggregated into mass,
distributing on the head, tail andmargin of thefilm.Whereas,fewer neoplastic cells or their groups are
present in funicular arrangement andmixedwithmormal marrow cells so that they can be easily
neglected when it is hyperplastic.Granulocytesoften contain toxicparticles andvacuoles.Megakaryocytes
may be increseased with maturation interruption,and also may be decreased or absent.Fragmented
erythrocytes such as helmet or triangular cells can be seen.
The most frequent neoplastic cells in bone marrow are divided as following threekinds:
1.Squamous cell carcinoma:It is originated from epithelium tissue,most frequently occurs in skin
eyes,earsnose,throat,ral cavity,utrine cervix,sophagus and penis,tc.he cells arecharacterid
by their big sizes.They are 15m~90 μm in diameter.Most cells are scattered,few ofwhich gather into
clumps.The cells display pleomorphism such as round,irregular,tadpole-shaped and snake-shaped.The
nuclei arelarge in size and round or ellipticin shape,and frequently located in thecenter ofcells and
Occasionally placed eccentrically.The chromatin is abundant and deeply stained,presenting with coarse
granules or clumps. The nuclear membranes are thick and the nucleoli are generally indistinct.The
cytoplasmis abundantandeosinophilicwithvacuolessometimes.
2.Adenocarcinoma:Itisusuallyoriginatedfromvariouskindsofglandsin thebody.Theadenocarcinomic
cells aremainlycharacterizedbygland-likelumen orpapilla-shaped arrangementandindistinct cellular
borderlines.The cells are large, about 17pm~26μm in diameter and is round or columelliform in shape.
They are identical in shape and size. Large nuclei are usually placed eccentrically with granular
chromatin and distinct nucleoli.The cytoplasm is scanty and stained blue,occasionally with obvious
mucous vacuoles which is present in signet-ring cell carcinoma.
3.Undifferentiated small cell carcinoma:The cancer cells come from the basal layer of squamous or
pillar epithelium with low differentiation and high malignancy.The main characteristics include zonal or
funiculus arrangement of the cells and clumps of aggregating cells.The cells are small and elliptic or
and deeplystained.Generally thenucleoliareabsent andmost cellshavelittlecytoplasm

骨髓坏死
骨髓坏死（Bonemarrownecrosis）常发生于累及骨髓的肿瘤性疾病、炎症和镰状细胞性贫血。主要临床
表现是骨骼疼痛，多见于脊柱、骨盆和四肢。其次为发热，进行性贫血和/或出血，外周血可见到幼粒、幼红细胞。
血象可有不同程度的贫血。白细胞计数正常或增高，分类可见幼粒细胞和幼红细胞。血小板常减少，少数
病例亦可正常。网织红细胞偏高或正常。
骨髓象髓液外观深棕色或呈灰色。其特征是大部分有核细胞溶解，细胞边缘模糊，形态分辨不清，重者只
剩染成粉红色的细胞痕迹。涂片背景上，溶解的细胞间呈均匀嗜酸性，偶尔中间夹杂有少许完整的幼红和幼粒细
胞，也可发现转移癌细胞。
Bone Marrow Necrosis
Bone marrow necrosis often occurs inneoplastic diseases involvingbone marrow,inflammation and
sickle cell anemia.Clinical manifestation is Themainly skeletal painwhich frequently present in vertebral
column,pelvis and limbs.Other symptoms include fever,progressive anemia and/or hemorrhage.Imma-
ture granulocytes and erythroblasts can be found in the peripheral blood.
Hemogram The severity of anemia is varying.Leukocyte count is normal or elevated.Immature
granulocytes and erythroblasts can be seen.Platelet count is usually decreased,and occasionally normal
ina few cases.Reticulocyte count is alittlehigh or normal.
ofmost nucleated cells. The borders of the cells are indistinct and the shapes are undistinguished.In
severe cases,only pink cellular trace can be seen.In the background of the smear,evenly-distributed
eosinophilic substance appears among the lyticcells,occasionally mixed with a couple of complete
erythroblasts and immature granulocytes.Metastastic carcinoma cells can be found.

神经母细胞瘤骨髓转移
神经母细胞瘤（Neuroblastoma）是由未成熟的神经母细胞构成的恶性肿瘤。多发生在4岁以前婴幼儿，原
四肢骨骼疼痛，腹胀并可触及包块，出现贫血和消瘦等。
血象红细胞明显减少。白细胞增加，偶可降低，分类时可见各阶段幼稚粒细胞，并可见幼红细胞。
一致，浆少呈蓝色。核为圆形，染色质细致，核仁不清。易见退化细胞，常误认为原始淋巴细胞。
Neuroblastoma Metastatic to Bone Marrow
commonly occurrs ininfants and toddllers under 4years.Primarypathogenic site is usuallylocated in the
medulla of the adrenal glands or their adjacent sympathicnervous system.Neuroblastoma has a high
malignancy andrapid progression and leads to early metastasis. General symptoms include fever,
headache,bone pain of limbs, abdominal distension with touchable mass,anemia and emaciation,etc.
Hemogram Erythrocytes are significantly decreased.Leukocytes are increased,but occasionally
decreased.Immature granulocytes in all differential stages and erythroblasts can be seen.
MyelogramHyperplasia of nucleated cells is present.Instead ofnormal cells the neoplastic cells are
scattered or gathered into mass.The cells areround and small in identical size.The cytoplasm is scanty
visible andoften misdiagnosed aslymphoblasts.

瘤细胞较密集，外形不规则。胞浆量少，嗜碱。胞核大小

红斑狼疮细胞
红斑狼疮细胞（Lupuserythematosuscell，LEcell）系红斑狼疮因子作用于成熟粒细胞和单核细胞，使胞
核溶解、膨胀，形成圆形均匀体，染成粉红色，称均匀体。均匀体被多个完整的中性粒细胞围绕形似花簇，称LE
细胞花团簇期。如果中性粒细胞吞噬了均匀体，中性粒细胞胞核被挤向一侧，则称为LE细胞。典型LE细胞的
均匀体必须失去胞核原来结构而均匀一致。即使如此，LE细胞也不是系统性红斑狼疮的特异所见，其他疾病也
可出现。
Lupus Erythematosus Cell
Lupus erythematosus cell (LE cell is a round homogeneous mass,which are stained pink and called
homogeneous mass, formed by the lysis and swelling of the nuclei resulted from the action of lupus
erythematosus factor on mature granulocytes and monocytes.The homogeneous mass is surrounded by
many complete neutrophils appearing as a rosette,that is called LE cell in rosette stage.The neutrophil
139
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
that has phagocytosed a homogeneous mass is called LE cell, in which the nucleus is jostled to one pole.
Homogeneous mass of typical LE cell must loss the primary nuclear structure and looks homogeneous.
Even this,LE cell is nota specific presentation of systemic lupus erythematosus and can appear in other
diseases as well.

郎格罕斯细胞性组织细胞增多症
郎格罕斯细胞性组织细胞增多症（Langerhanscellhistiocytosis,LCH）是一组原因未明的组织细胞增生
性疾病。多见于2岁以下婴幼儿，故又称婴儿型组织细胞症。临床表现多有持续性发热、贫血，肝脾明显肿大伴
淋巴结肿大。皮肤常受累，多为出血性斑丘疹。
血象贫血较明显，红细胞常<2.0×102/L，为正细胞正色素性贫血。白细胞大致正常，少数病儿可>20.0×
10°/L，也可减低，偶见幼粒、幼红细胞。血小板正常或减少。
骨髓象非充脂性的组织细胞增多，胞体椭圆形、不规则形或多角形。核圆形或肾形，常偏在。胞浆内含有
被吞噬的颗粒、红细胞或白细胞。
皮疹印片检查组织细胞形态同骨髓象，尚可见到少数含脂类的泡沫样组织细胞，对诊断有重要价值。
Langerhans Cell Histiocytosis
Langerhans cell histiocytosis (LCH) is a histiocytic proliferative disease of unknown origin.The
disease affects neonates and infants under 2years old,so it is also called infant histiocytosis.The most
common clinicalmanifestations arepersistent fever and anemia,marked hepatosplenomegaly accompanied
by lymphadenopathy.Skin involvement is frequently presentingwith hemorrhagicmaculopapule.
HemogramMarked normocytic-normochromicanemia occurs frequently with erythrocytesless
than 2.0x10/L.Leukocytes are almost normal,but may be more than 20.0x10/Lin a few patients
or decreased.Occasionally immature granulocytes and erythroblasts can be found.Platelets are normal or
decreased.
Myelogram Non-adipose histiocytes are increased and elliptic,irregular or poly-angled in shape.
The nuclei are round or reniformed,and usually placedeccentrically.The cytoplasm is engorged with
phagocytosedgranules,erythrocytesandleukocytes.
Skin Rash Smear The morphous of histiocytes is the same as that in bone marrow.In addition,a
fewfoaminghistiocytes containing lipids can be seen,which has an importantvalue in the diagnosis.

尼曼-匹克病
尼曼-匹克病（Niemann-Pickdisease）又称神经磷脂病，是一组少见的脂质代谢障碍性疾病。其特点是
单核-巨噬细胞系统和其他组织的细胞中有神经磷脂和胆固醇的聚集。大多为婴儿发病，主要症状是营养不良和
发育迟缓、贫血、肝脾迅速肿大伴淋巴结肿大、腹部膨隆，也可有耳聋或失明。本病可分A、B及C三型。A型
及B型为酸性鞘磷酶（Acidsphingomyelinase，ASM）缺乏所致，C型为细胞内低密度脂蛋白胆固醇的转运缺
陷所致。
血象常有中度贫血。白细胞总数增高，也可减少，淋巴细胞、单核细胞乃至中性粒细胞胞浆中可见数个类
脂质性空泡，对诊断本病有参考意义。血小板正常，晚期则降低。
骨髓象骨髓中有特征性的尼曼-匹克细胞。这种细胞呈圆形、椭圆形或多角形，直径20~90um。核较小，
圆形或椭圆形，偏在，常为一个，亦可见2个。胞浆中充满泡沫状脂肪颗粒，呈蜂窝状，经美蓝一伊红染色后呈
浅蓝色。
Niemann-Pick Disease
Niemann-Pick disease,which isa less common lipid storage disorder,is also called sphingomyelin
disease.It is characterized by the accumulation of sphingomyelin and/or cholesterol in the mono-
macrophages and cells of other tissues,which has a higher incidence in infants.Major clinical manifes-
tations present with dystrophia and development retardation,anemia,rapid enlargement of the liver and
spleen accompanied bylymphadenopathy andabdominal eminence,occasionally with blindness and
deafness.The disease canbe divided into three types.TypeA andBisresulted from acid sphingomyelinase
deficiency.Type Cresultsfrom defective cholesterol transport in the cells.
HemogramModerate anemia is frequently present. WBC count may be increased or decreased.
Several adipoidvacuoles may be presentin the cytoplasm of lymphocytes,monocytes and even neutro-
philic granulocytes,which has a referential significance in diagnosis.Platelets are normal and decreased
in thelate stage.
MyelogramThe appearance of Nimann-Pick cells is specific for the diagnosis. The cells are round,
ellipticorpoly-angled with 20pm~90μm indiameter.Single or twonucleiare small,round orelliptic,
andplacedeccentrically.The cytoplasm is full of foaming fatgranules,giving honeycomb appearance and
stained light blue by methylene blue-eosin.

戈谢病
戈谢病（Gaucherdisease）是一种类脂质代谢异常性疾病，为常染色体隐性遗传。急性型多见于婴幼儿、病
情进展迅速，除肝脾肿大外常有神经系统症状，如两眼内斜、角弓反张等，常在2岁前死亡。慢性病例多为青年
或成年人，最突出的表现为脾脏肿大伴贫血，肝脏可轻度肿大。晚期皮肤黏膜有出血，皮肤有黄棕色色素沉着。
血象常呈中度贫血，为正细胞正色素性。白细胞常减少，血小板轻度降低。
骨髓象除有脾功能亢进的骨髓象外，以戈谢细胞浸润最具特征性。它是含有葡萄糖脑苷脂的巨噬细胞，胞
体较大，直径约20～80um，圆形、椭圆形或多角形。胞浆量多，淡蓝色，含有许多波浪状条索纤维，有时浆中
有吞噬的血细胞。核小，常为1~2个，偶达3～4个，偏在。染色质粗，有时浓集成块，偶见1~2个核仁。
Gaucher Disease
Gaucher disease isa disorderofabnormaladipoidmetabolismwhichisinherited asautosomal
recessive traits.Acute type of the disease frequently occurs in early infancy with rapid progression,
hepatosplenomegaly,fulminatingneurologicsymptoms such as oculomotor abnormalities and opisthotonus.
The patientsusually diewithin 2years of theirlife.Chronic cases mainly occurs in theyoung or adults.
The mostpredominantmanifestationspresentwith splenomegaly accompaniedby anemia.Slightheptomegaly
may exist.In thelate stage,hemorrhage of the skin andmucosa andyellow-brown pigmentation in the
skin may be present
HemogramAmoderatenormocyticandnormochromaticanemia isfrequently present.wBCcount
isusually decreased.Platelet countis decreased mildly.
MyelogramBesides the findings of hypersplenism,the infiltration of Gaucher cells is the most
specific.Gaucher cells are the macrophages containing glucocerebroside.They are big and 20μm ~80μm
in diameter.The cells are round,elliptic or poly-angled in shape.The light blue cytoplasm is abundant
with many waving fibers and ingested erythrocytes occasionally.The nuclei are small and placed
eccentrically.The number of the nuclei is usually 1~2, and occasionally 3~4.The chromatin is coarse
andgathered into clumps.Occasionally1~2nucleoli can be seen.

海蓝组织细胞增生症
海蓝组织细胞增生症（Sea-bluehistiocytosis）是一种很少见的脂质代谢异常性疾病。有原发性和获得
性之分，但需除外继发因素。本病的特点是：肝脾肿大，淋巴结肿大少见；血小板减少伴轻微紫癜；骨髓中
出现较多海蓝组织细胞。
血象轻度贫血，白细胞减少。几乎所有病例血小板均减少。
骨髓象可见较多的海蓝组织细胞。它是一种巨噬细胞，呈圆形或椭圆形，直径20~60μm。胞浆极丰富，
充满了海蓝色或蓝绿色颗粒。常有一个细胞核，偶见2个，呈圆形或椭圆形，偏在，核染色质深染呈块状。偶有
一个核仁。
Sea-Blue Histiocytosis
Sea-bluehistiocytosisis ararelipid storage disorder.It can be dividedintoprimary andacquired
types when the secondary factors are excluded.The disease presentswithhepatosplenomegaly,thromb
144
图谱
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOG
nodes is rare.
Hemogram
Mild anemia,leukocytopenia,and thrombocytopeniaare foundin almost all cases.
MyelogramMany sea-blue cells ispresent.Sea-blue cellsarea kind ofmacrophageswhich are
round or ellipticand20μm~60μm indiameter.Thecytoplasm isveryabundant,filled withsea-blue
or blue-green granules. The cells usually possess one nucleus and occasionally two nuclei,which are
roundor ellipticandplaced eccentrically with deeply stained chromatin clumps.Occasionallyone
nucleolus can be found.

正常淋巴结
正常淋巴结的细胞约85%为成熟淋巴细胞，10%为幼稚淋巴细胞，5%为原始淋巴细胞，偶见网状细胞和浆
细胞等。此外，尚可看到组织细胞、巨噬细胞等。
Normal Lymph Node
Nearly 85%of the cellsin normal lymph nodes are mature lymphocytes,10% are immature
lymphocytes,5%are lymphoblasts.Reticular cells and plasmocytes canbe seen occasionally.Moreover,
histiocytes and macrophages and so on can also be seen.

急性淋巴结炎
急性淋巴结炎（Acutelymphadenitis）时，肿大的淋巴结硬度中等，重者可有明显的红、肿、热、痛伴有
发热、白细胞增高等临床表现。
淋巴结涂片有核细胞丰富，可见散在的吞噬型组织细胞。中性粒细胞明显增多并伴有退形性变，表现为胞
核肿胀，细胞界限不清，胞浆中有中毒颗粒和空泡等。涂片背景为无结构的染成粉红色的物质。
Acute Lymphadenitis
In acute lymphadenitis,the swellinglymphnodes aremoderately hard.Severe patientspresent with
obviously red,swelling,hot and painful lymph nodes accompanied byfever and leukocytosis.
Lymphaden SmearNucleated cells are abundant.Phagocytic-type histiocytes are scattered.Neutro-
phils increase obviously with degeneration,representingas swelling nuclei,unclear cell boundaries,and
toxicparticles and vacuolesin the cytoplasm.Therearepinkstructureless substance in the background
of the smear.

淋巴结结核
淋巴结结核（Lymphadentuberculosis）最常见的是颈部淋巴结结核。初期肿大的淋巴结质地较软，无痛，
可推动。继之淋巴结相互粘连，融合成块。晚期发生干酪样坏死、液化、破溃，最终形成经久不愈的窦道。病人
可有低热、盗汗、消瘦等结核中毒症状。淋巴结结核可分为增殖型（涂片可见郎罕细胞及上皮样细胞）及干酪型。
Lymphaden Tuberculosis
Tuberculosis occuringin theneck lymph nodes is themostcommon type of lymphaden tuberculosis
In the early stage,the swellinglymphadens are soft,painless andunfixed to touch.Then the lymphadens
adhere to each other and agglomerate together into mass.In the advanced stage, caseous necrosis,
liquification and eruption of the lymphaden occur,forming irrecoverable sinus tract finally.The patients
may experience toxic symptoms of tuberculosis,such as low-grade fever,night sweats,weight loss and
soon.Lymphaden tuberculosis can be divided intoproliferation type(Langerhanscells and epithelioid
cells can be seen in the smear) and caseous type.

霍奇金病
霍奇金病（Hodgkindisease，HD）是淋巴瘤的一种。多见于青年，主要症状是颈部淋巴结无痛性、慢性、
进行性肿大。当深部淋巴结肿大时压迫邻近器官引起相应的症状，约1/6病人有周期性发热（Pel-Ebstein热），
有时周身瘙痒可为本病的唯一症状。10%左右的病人脾脏肿大，肝实质受累时肝区疼痛伴肝脏肿大，少数病人可
有黄痘。有时并发自身免疫性溶血性贫血。大多数瘤细胞CD15，CD30，CD45，B和T细胞抗原大多为阴性，
少数病例T细胞和B细胞相关抗原即使表达也很微弱的。
血象可有轻中度贫血。白细胞计数有时轻度升高，中性粒细胞增多、淋巴细胞相对减少，约20%病例嗜
酸性粒细胞增多。网织红细胞正常或减少，伴发自身免疫性溶血性贫血时增高。血小板一般正常。外周血涂片有
时可找到霍奇金细胞（里-斯细胞）。
骨髓象一般无特异性改变，如能找到典型里-斯（Reed-Sternberg，R-S）细胞，对诊断有帮助。R-S细
胞胞体约25～50um，胞浆丰富，可为嗜双色性或略嗜碱性。有巨大双核，呈“镜影”状排列，简称镜影细胞。
本病时骨髓细胞学检查R-S细胞阳性只占3%，故淋巴结检查对诊断帮助更大。

Hodgkin disease
Hodgkin disease(HD) is a kind of lymphomas and commonly occurs in theyoung people. The most
frequent symptom is chronic and progressive painless lymphadenectasis in the neck.The oppression of
contiguous organs by deep and swellinglymphadens induces the corresponding symptoms.Cyclic fever
(Pel-Ebstein fever)presents in about 1/6patients. Sometimes generalized pruritus can be the only
symptom of the disease.Splenomegaly presents innearly 10%of thepatients.Pain in the hepaticregion
with hepatomegaly ocurs when liver parenchyma is involved.A few patients have jaundice.The disease
is complicated by autoimmune hemolyticanemia sometimes.Most tumor cells express CD15 and CD30,
and donot express CD45,B-cell or T-cell antigens.In several cases,the tumor cells can slightly express
B-cell or T-cell antigens.
HemogramSlightormoderate anemia canpresent.Leukocytecountelevatesslightly sometimes
withincreasedneutrophilicgranulocytesandrelatively decreased lymphocytes.Eosinophilicgranulocytes
increase in about20%ofcases.Reticulocyte count isnormal or decreased,butincreasedwhen complicated
by autoimmune hemolytic anemia.Platelets are usually normal.Hodgkin cells (Reed-Sternberg cells)
sometimes are shown in the smear.
MyelogramUsually no specific change is detected.It will be helpful for the diagnosis to find
typical Reed-Sternberg（R-S)cells.R-Scells is about 25μm~50μm,with abundant cytoplasm which
canbebicolor-phile or slightly basophilic.There aregiant conjugatenuclei in the cells showingmirror
image appearance,so called mirror image cells for short.Because the positive rate of R-S cellsin marrow
cytomorphologicexaminationis only3%,lymphnodebiopsyismoreusefulfor thediagnosis.

非霍奇金淋巴瘤
非霍奇金淋巴瘤（Non-HodgkinLymphoma，NHL），常以颈部无痛性淋巴结肿大为首发症状，咽淋巴结
环（韦氏咽环）、胃肠道及腹腔淋巴结病变较霍奇金病多见。若纵隔、腹膜后和肠系膜等处的淋巴结肿大时可产
生相应的压迫症状。约有1/3~1/2病人骨髓受累，当骨髓中出现大量淋巴肉瘤细胞形成白血病样改变时，称为
白血肉瘤（Leukosarcoma），又称淋巴肉瘤细胞白血病。可有发热、盗汗、体重减轻等症状。
血象疾病初期白细胞总数大多正常，而淋巴细胞增多或相对增多，晚期时白细胞减少。约20%的原淋巴
细胞型淋巴瘤在晚期并发白血病，其血象与急性淋巴细胞白血病相差无儿。晚期约半数病人有不同程度的贫血和
血小板减少。
骨髓象早期无特征性改变，晚期时淋巴瘤细胞侵犯骨髓者近20%。
Non-Hodgkin Lymphoma
Non-Hodgkin Lymphoma (NHL),usually takes painless lymphadenectasis in the neck as the first
symptom.Lymphadenopathyinlymphonoduspharyngealisring(Waldeyer tonsillar ring),gastrointestinal
tractand abdominalcavityaremorecommoninnon-HodgkinLymphoma.Lymphadenectasisinmediastinum,
retroperitoneum or mesentery and so on may result in corresponding oppression symptoms.Bonemarrow
involvementpresentsinabout1/3~1/2patients.Itiscalledleukosarcomaorlymphosarcomaleukemia
that a number of lymphosarcoma cells appears in bone marrow showing leukemic“phase”.Some
s
HemogramLeukocyte count is usually normal in the early stage of the disease with increased or
comparatively increased lymphocytes.Leukocytesdecreasein thelate stage.Nearly20%of lymphoblastic
lymphoma are complicated byleukemia in the advanced stage,for which thehemogram isnearly the
same as that of acute lymphocyticleukemia (ALL).In the advanced stage,anemia and thrombocytopenia
invarious degrees may present in nearly half of the patients.
Myelogram In the early stage no specific change can be found. Bone marrow is infiltrated by
lymphomacellsinnearly20%ofthepatients inthelatestage.

Sezary综合征
原发于皮肤的T淋巴细胞，是非霍奇金淋巴瘤的特殊类型。好发于40～60岁。无性别差异。其特点是，泛
发性红皮病，伴水肿，时间长的皮肤浸润增厚，色素沉着，剧痒，毛发脱落。
血象白细胞中度增加（10~30）×10/L，也可更高。Sezary细胞（SC）大小不一，胞浆由浅蓝到中等
蓝色，量少，偶见嗜天青颗粒和空泡。核呈脑回状，核仁不清。约占白细胞总数的5%~26%，糖原染色阳性，血
红蛋白及血小板大致正常。
骨髓象骨髓有核细胞增生明显活跃，早期SC数量少，晚期可增高，粒红两系随之相应减少。
Sezary Syndrome
The disease is primarily originated from cutaneous T lymphocytes and is a special type ofnon-
Hodgkin lymphoma.It more frequently occurs in the patients aged 40~60without difference in sex.It
is characterized by diffused erythroderma following edema,infiltration and incrassation of the skin,
156
图谐
实用血液学细胞学图谱ATLASOFPRACTICALHAEMATOLOGYANDCYTOLOGY
pigmentation,tempestuously itch and depilation.
HemogramWhite blood cells increase inmoderate degree,are(10~30)x10/Lorhigher.Sezary cells
(SC) are varying in size.The scanty cytoplasm is stained from light blue tomedium blue,occasionallywith
azurophilic granules and vacuoles.The nuclei are gyrus-shapedwith unclear nucleoli.The cells are26%of
totalwhite blood cells and arePAS stainingpositive.Hemoglobin and platelets are normal.
MyelogramThe marrow ismarkedly hypercellular.Sezary cell countmay be low in the early stage,
but it will increase in the late stage,followed by the decrease of granulocytic and erythrocytic series.

淋巴结转移瘤
肿瘤细胞由原发部位转移到淋巴结时，称淋巴结转移瘤（Lymphadenmetastatictumor），其中以转移癌
最常见。除恶性黑色素瘤外，一般从形态学上无法确定原发灶。临床表现常具有原发肿瘤的相应症状，淋巴结肿
大、进展较快、质地坚硬是其特点，晚期时淋巴结比较固定。
Lymphaden Metastatic Tumors
It iscalled lymphadenmetastatic tumor thatneoplasticcellsmetastasizefrom the original focus tothe
lymphaden,of which metastatic carcinoma is the most common.Usually the original tumors can not be
identifiedmorphologically except malignantmelanoma.The clinicalmanifestationsusuallypresentwith
some symptomsoftheprimarytumorsandarecharacterizedbytherapidenlargementofhardlymph
nodes.In the advanced stage the lymphadens are comparatively fixed.

纤维肉瘤淋巴结转移
纤维肉瘤（Fibrosarcoma）是恶性间叶性肿瘤中最常见的一种，以四肢皮下组织或深部组织为多。肉眼观察
其切面均质细腻如鱼肉状，故称肉瘤。
Lymphaden Metastasis of Fibrosarcoma
Fibrosarcoma is the most common type in malignant lobus intermedius tumors.It often occurs in
hypodermia of extremities or tissues in deeppart of thebody.It is called sarcoma because its cross section
lookshomogenousand exquisitejustlikefishwhenobservedbynaked eyes.

黑色素瘤淋巴结转移
恶性黑色素瘤（Malignantmelanoma）常系色素痣恶变而来，故凡黑痣迅速扩大，颜色显著加深的均应疑

Malignant melanoma usuallyresults from the cancerationofpigmentednevus.Thus thisdisease
should always be suspectedif melanoticnevus expandsrapidly and deepens conspicuously.Melanoma
usuallyprogressesrapidly andmetastasizes distantly earlier.Thelymphaden aspiration fluid lookspuce.

宫颈癌淋巴结转移
宫颈癌（Uterinecervixcancer）多见于30~60岁妇女。临床表现主要有性交后出血或白带增多，晚
期出现贫血、消瘦、白带奇臭及阴道不规则出血。本病以鳞状细胞癌最为常见。
Lymphaden Metastasis of Uterine Cervix Cancer
Uterine cervix cancer mostly occursin women aged from30 to 60years.The clinicalmanifestations
arecommonlybleedingand increased leucorrhea aftercoitus.Anemia,weightloss,smelly leucorrhea and
irregular bleeding ofvaginapresent in the late stage.Squamous cell carcinoma is the most common in the
disease.

清，有大量空泡。核呈椭圆形或不规则形，大小悬殊，染
色质比较细致，核仁大，清晰，1至多个不等

nuclei are oval orirregularin shape and significantly
different in size.The chromatin is fine with one or

肺癌淋巴结转移
肺癌（Pulmonarycarcinoma）是常见恶性肿瘤之一，多发生于50~60岁，男性多于女性。临床表现有刺激
性干咳，少量或大量咯血，持续性胸痛，呼吸困难或气促，发热和阻塞性肺炎等。常伴有胸腔积液及锁骨上淋巴
结转移。细胞学检查可分为鳞癌、腺癌及未分化癌（大细胞型和小细胞型）。
Lymphaden Metastasis of Pulmonary Carcinoma
Pulmonary carcinoma isone ofthemost common malignant tumors.Thepatients are often 50~60
yearsold witha malepredominance.The clinicalmanifestationsinclude irritative tussiculation,slightor
severe hemoptysis,persistent chest pain,dyspnea,tachypnea,fever,obstructive pneumonia and so on.It
is usually complicated bypleural effusionand supraclavicular lymphaden metastasis.It is categorized on
the basis of cytological examination as squamous carcinoma,adenocarcinoma and undifferentiated carci
noma (big cell type and small cell type).

浆膜腔积液中组织细胞与间皮细胞
浆膜腔积液中常见有组织细胞、间皮细胞及淋巴细胞等。
1.组织细胞浆膜液中的单核细胞称为组织细胞，因此小型组织细胞颇似单核细胞，但形态变化较大。细
胞常呈不规则形，偶为圆形。胞浆灰色，常有伪足形成，可见少许紫红色细小颗粒和空泡。大型组织细胞常吞噬
血细胞及其碎片。核呈圆形、椭圆形、肾形或不规则形，有1~2个，染色质较疏松。大型组织细胞偶可见到核
仁。若浆中含有大空泡，核被挤向边缘而形成印戒状，也称印戒细胞。
2.间皮细胞来自浆膜表面的扁皮细胞，脱落后则呈圆形，散在或成簇。按其形态主要可分为两型。
①嗜碱性间皮细胞圆形或椭圆形。胞浆嗜碱蓝染，边缘清楚。核圆形或椭圆形，染色质细点状，较致密。
核仁14个不等。有时多个间皮细胞融合成细胞团。
②嗜酸性间皮细胞圆形或椭圆形。胞浆嗜酸淡红色，可见细小颗粒。核圆形或椭圆形，偏在，染色质致密。

Histiocytes and Mesothelial Cells in Serous Membrane Effusion
The histiocytes,mesothelial cells and lymphocytes are often seen in serousmembrane effusion.
1.HistiocytesThe monocytes in serosa effusion are called histiocytes,and small histiocytes are
similar tomonocytes.However,their appearances are obviously different.Histiocytes commonly appear
irregular,sometimes round.The cytoplasma is grey,usually with pseudopodia and a few fine purplish-
redgranulesandvacuoles.Bighistiocytesusually swallowblood cells and their fragments.There are 1
2nuclei,which are round,oval,reniformed or irregular with loose chromatin.The nucleoli can be
occasionally seen in big histiocytes.If the cell contains the cytoplasm with big vacuoles thenucleus is
squeezed to one side of the cell to form signet ring-like appearance,which is called signet-ring cell.
2.Mesothelial cellsThese cells are originated from flat epithelial cells in serosal surface,and fell off
to become spherical cells.They are usually scattered or in clusters.They can be divided into two types
dependingontheirmorphous.
①BasophilicmesothelialcellsThe cells areround or oval with basophilic,blue-stained cytoplasm
and have clear boundaries. The nuclei are round and oval with condensed and fine-punctiform chromatin.
Thenumberofnucleoli varies from 1to4.Sometimesseveralmesothelialcellsarefusedto formacell
clump.
Eosinophilicmesothelial cellsThe cells are usually round or oval with acidophiliclight-red
cytoplasm.There are fine granules in the cytoplasm.The nuclei are round,oval and eccentric with dense
chromatin.

浆膜嗜酸性粒细胞增多症
起病急缓不一。肺炎、自发性液气胸、恶性肿瘤及寄生虫性浆膜反应等可能是本病的原因。临床表现有胸痛、
咳嗽、呼吸困难及胸腔积液等症状和体征。胸腔积液常为草黄色，偶为血性。
EosinophilicGranulocytosis ofSerous Membrane
Thediseasecanhavea chronicoracuteonset.In etiology,pneumonia,spontaneoushydropneumothorax,
malignant tumors and parasites-induced serosalreactionmaybe the causes of the disease.Clinical
manifestations present with chest pain,cough,dyspnea and pleural effusion,etc.The pleural effusion is
usuallyyellow green.Hematodes effusion can occasionally be found.

恶性间皮瘤
间皮瘤（Mesotheliomas）来源于胸膜、腹膜、心包等浆膜腔表面的间皮组织。局限性者多为良性，弥漫性
者均为恶性。本病多发生于中年，男性多于女性。腹膜间皮瘤主要的临床表现是消瘦、腹胀、腹痛、腹部包块及
腹水。
Malignant Mesotheliomas
Mesotheliomas are originated from themesothelial tissue in the surface of serous membrane such as
pleura,peritoneum and pericardium,etc.Localized mesotheliomas are usually benign,while thewide-
spread ones are all malignant. The disease mostly occurs in the middle aged men.Main clinical
manifestations of theperitoneum mesothelioma are weightloss,abdominaldistension or pain,abdominal
mass and ascites.

肝细胞癌
原发性肝癌（Primarylivercancer）（包括肝细胞和胆管上皮细胞癌）为我国常见的恶性肿瘤之一。起病
隐匿，进展迅速，病死率高。发病年龄以40~50岁多见，男性多于女性。
临床表现：肝区疼痛，多呈持续性胀痛或钝痛；食欲不振，食后腹胀，乏力，消瘦，全身衰弱；发热，可
持续性低热或弛张热；肝脏进行性肿大，质地坚硬，表面有大小不等的结节或巨块，边缘不规则。
Hepatocellular carcinoma
Primary liver cancer (includinghepatocellular carcinoma and epithelial cell carcinoma)is one of the
most commonmalignant carcinomas in our country.The disease has an insidious onset,rapid progression
and high mortality.The patients from 40 to 50 years are common,and more in male than in female.
Clinical manifestations:The patients usually presentwith persistent distending or dull pain in the
hepaticregion,anorexia,abdominal distension after meal,fatigue,weight loss,weakness,persistant low
grade fever or remittent fever,and progresive hepatomegaly.The liver solid and irregular at the edge,
having touchable nodus or large clumps in different size on the surface.
图341肝癌穿刺涂片

有的边缘部染淡紫红色，境界不清，有空泡。胞核椭圆形
或不规则形，染色质颗粒不均匀。核仁数目不清，有空泡

胃
癌
胃癌（Gastriccarcinoma）是消化道最常见的肿瘤。早期症状轻微或无症状，一经诊断大多已到中晚期。表
现为食欲不振、食后胀饱、贫血、体重下降和上腹部疼痛等。上腹部偏右侧的肿块为主要体征。
Gastric Carcinoma
Gastric carcinoma is the most common in digestive tract tumors.In the early stage of the disease the
patientshave slightsymptoms orare asymptomatic.Thediseaseisusuallyin theadvancedstage at the
time of diagnosis.The symptoms include anorexia,abdominal distention after meal,anemia,weight loss,
